  6. 06
    NiPS3 中 Zhang-Rice 三重态的微观证据#
    Microscopic evidence for a Zhang-Rice triplet state in the van der Waals antiferromagnet, NiPS₃#
    📊 含图深析
    🧭 物理 / 凝聚态📖 arXiv / cond-mat👤 Beom Hyun Kim, Youjin Lee, Junik Hwang, Junghyun Kim, Je-Geun Park, Seung-Ho Baek🔥 AI 83

    💡 亮点：NiPS3 的磁激子被指认为 Zhang-Rice 三重态相关。

    📖 展开分析 + 配图
    研究问题NiPS₃ 中低温极窄磁激子为何具有异常相干性？其背后的局域基态到底是普通 Ni²⁺ d⁸ 局域自旋，还是包含硫配体空穴、Ni 3d–S 3p 强杂化的 Zhang-Rice triplet 自旋-电荷纠缠态？
    创新方法利用 ³³S 富集 NiPS₃ 单晶的 ³³S NMR 直接“照亮”硫配体轨道，并与 ³¹P NMR 形成双核对照：³³S 作为带四极矩的配体探针同时感受 S 3p 自旋密度与 EFG/电荷涨落，³¹P 主要感受 Ni 3d 磁矩；二者 Knight shift 同步但弛豫行为相反，成为识别 Zhang-Rice triplet 的关键 Aha 点。
    工作流程输入 ³³S 富集 NiPS₃ 单晶 → 在 5.93 T、150–320 K 顺磁相中采集角度/温度依赖 ³³S NMR 谱 → 拟合二阶四极谱线得到 νQ、η 与 EFG 方向 → 提取 ³³S Knight shift 并与 ³¹P Knight shift、体磁化率做 K–χ 分析 → 测量 ³³S/³¹P 核自旋-晶格弛豫率 T₁⁻¹ → 用 R₁=(T₁χT)⁻¹ 分离动力学贡献 → 输出 p-d 杂化 ZRT 基态与临界向列电荷涨落图像。
    关键结果³³S 谱显示异常强四极相互作用，νQ = 6.4 MHz、η = 0.1，EFG 主轴位于 ab 面内，指向硫周围强烈面内电荷不对称；³³S 与 ³¹P Knight shift 均在约 250 K 出现宽峰并跟随磁化率，但 ³³Ahf = 44.2 kOe/μB，远大于 ³¹Ahf = −1.8 kOe/μB，证明 S 3p 上存在显著转移自旋密度；³³S 弛豫率在 Tₙ = 155 K 附近幂律发散，³³R₁ ∝ |T−T₀|⁻⁰·⁴⁶⁴，T₀ = 152 K，而 ³¹P 不发散，说明临界涨落来自硫位点电荷/EFG 与向列相关，而非普通自旋临界涨落。
    应用价值该研究为 NiPS₃ 的磁激子相干性提供局域微观基础：硫配体空穴与镍磁矩形成统一 Zhang-Rice triplet，自旋、轨道、电荷和向列涨落被纳入同一图像；这为设计具有长寿命磁激子、强自旋-电荷耦合和可调向列性的二维范德华量子材料提供实验判据与材料路线。

    第一部分：核心概览（Overview）

    NiPS₃ 中磁激子的异常相干性长期缺乏微观解释。利用 ³³S 富集单晶的 ³³S NMR，结合既有 ³¹P NMR，直接探测硫配体轨道上的自旋与电荷动力学，给出 Zhang-Rice triplet（ZRT）基态的微观证据：硫 3p 轨道存在显著转移自旋密度，并与镍 3d 磁矩形成统一的自旋三重态体系。³³S 弛豫率在 Tₙ = 155 K 附近呈幂律发散，而 ³¹P 不发散，指向与电荷转移耦合的临界向列涨落。该工作把 NiPS₃ 的磁激子、强 p-d 杂化、配体空穴、自旋-电荷纠缠和向列性统一到同一微观图像中。

    ---

    第二部分：结构化快速回顾

    《Microscopic evidence for a Zhang-Rice triplet state in the van der Waals antiferromagnet, NiPS₃》（None，）

    背景

    NiPS₃ 是范德华反铁磁体，低于 Tₙ = 155 K 进入 zigzag 反铁磁序，并在有序相中表现出极窄的磁激子线宽，低温下约 0.4 meV。围绕该激子的本质已有 Zhang-Rice exciton、Hund’s exciton、triplet-singlet exciton、polaron exciton、spin-entangled exciton 等模型，但缺乏能区分基态量子纠缠构型的局域实验证据。

    方法

    制备 ³³S 富集 NiPS₃ 单晶，采用 ³³S NMR 测量温度、角度依赖谱线、Knight shift 与核自旋-晶格弛豫率。外场 5.93 T，温度范围 150–320 K，样品尺寸 3 × 2 × 0.2 mm³。通过与 ³¹P NMR 对比，区分 Ni 自旋涨落与 S 位点电荷 / EFG 涨落。

    结果

    ³³S 谱线显示强二阶四极相互作用，拟合得到 νQ = 6.4 MHz，η = 0.1。³³S Knight shift 与 ³¹P Knight shift 温度依赖一致，均跟随体磁化率，在约 250 K 附近出现宽峰。K–χ 拟合得到 ³³Ahf = 44.2 kOe/μB，远大于 ³¹Ahf = −1.8 kOe/μB，说明 S 3p 轨道上存在异常高自旋密度。³³S 弛豫率在接近 Tₙ 时发散，归一化弛豫率满足 ³³R₁ ∝ |T − T₀|⁻⁰·⁴⁶⁴，其中 T₀ = 152 K。

    讨论

    ³³S 与 ³¹P 的 Knight shift 一致性说明 S 3p 配体空穴与 Ni 3d 磁矩构成统一自旋系统。NiPS₃ 基态更适合描述为 d⁸ 与 d⁹L̲ 构型叠加的 p-d 杂化自旋三重态，即 Zhang-Rice triplet。³³S 弛豫发散而 ³¹P 不发散，排除了普通临界自旋涨落，指向 S 位点 EFG / 电荷涨落，进一步关联到由 Ni–Ni 键自旋相关函数驱动的向列涨落。

    局限

    NMR 信号在 Tₙ 以下因磁性展宽而消失，因此直接测量仅限顺磁相。向列长程序在体材料中尚未被直接观测，³³S 弛豫发散被解释为二维层内向列临界涨落而非已确立的体向列相。Supplemental 中的超精细张量和角度拟合细节未在正文完全展开。

    结论

    NiPS₃ 的局域电子结构不是简单局域 Ni²⁺ d⁸ 图像，而是包含显著 d⁹L̲ 配体空穴成分的 Zhang-Rice triplet。该 ZRT 基态提供磁激子相干性、自旋-电荷耦合、异常四极相互作用和临界向列涨落的共同微观基础。

    ---

    第三部分：逐章节冷凝解析（Section-by-Section Condensing）

    Title

    Zhang-Rice triplet is the central microscopic claim

    标题直接把研究焦点锁定为 Zhang-Rice triplet state，并强调证据层级为 microscopic evidence，即不是仅从光谱现象或理论拟合推断，而是通过局域核磁探针识别 NiPS₃ 中的配体空穴、自旋密度与低能涨落。标题原文为 *"Microscopic evidence for a Zhang-Rice triplet state in the van der Waals antiferromagnet, NiPS₃"*，其中 van der Waals antiferromagnet 指出材料平台是层状弱层间耦合反铁磁体。

    ---

    Abstract

    Quantum-entangled states are experimentally hard to identify

    研究出发点是固体中量子纠缠态的直接识别极其困难。摘要开篇指出，量子纠缠态是量子材料涌现现象的基础，但实验确认仍是难题：*"Quantum-entangled states underpin many emergent phenomena in quantum materials, yet their direct experimental identification remains a challenge."* 这里的挑战并非简单观测某个激发，而是识别其背后的多体基态构型。

    NiPS₃ hosts a resolution-limited magnetic exciton and is a candidate for a Zhang-Rice triplet

    NiPS₃ 的关键异常现象是磁有序相中的 resolution-limited magnetic exciton，即线宽受仪器分辨率限制，暗示极长寿命和强相干性。摘要明确指出：*"NiPS₃, a van der Waals antiferromagnet exhibiting a resolution-limited magnetic exciton in its ordered phase, has been proposed to host a many-body entangled Zhang-Rice triplet state."* 该表述把磁激子与 many-body entangled ZRT 联系起来。

    ³³S NMR provides direct local evidence for charge-transfer character

    核心实验是对 ³³S 富集 NiPS₃ 单晶进行 ³³S NMR。摘要给出最重要结论：*"using ³³S nuclear magnetic resonance (NMR) on ³³S-enriched NiPS₃ single crystals, we provide microscopic evidence for this charge-transfer state."* 由于硫是配体位点，³³S NMR 对 S 3p 配体空穴和局域 EFG 极其敏感，能够检验 d⁸ 与 d⁹L̲ 混合。

    ³³S and ³¹P Knight shifts reveal a unified spin-triplet configuration

    摘要中的关键证据是 ³³S 与 ³¹P Knight shift 的温度依赖。二者显示共同局域自旋响应，说明 S 3p 与 Ni 3d 不是独立自由度，而是强杂化的同一三重态系统：*"The ³³S and ³¹P Knight shifts as a function of temperature reveal a unified spin-triplet configuration arising from strong hybridization between a self-doped hole in the S 3p orbitals and a hole in Ni 3d orbitals."* 这里 self-doped hole 表示无需外部掺杂即可在配体轨道上形成空穴。

    ³³S relaxation detects critical charge fluctuations near Tₙ

    ³³S 核自旋-晶格弛豫率在接近 Tₙ = 155 K 时出现幂律发散：*"the ³³S nuclear spin-lattice relaxation rate exhibits a power-law divergence as it approaches the Néel temperature Tₙ = 155 K"*。由于 ³³S 具有 I = 3/2 与四极矩，可耦合 EFG / 电荷涨落；这种发散被解释为集体电荷涨落的临界慢化：*"indicating critical slowing down of collective charge fluctuations consistent with spin-nematic correlations."*

    Spin-charge-intertwined ground state explains magnetic-exciton coherence

    摘要最终把 ZRT、配体电荷、自旋向列涨落与磁激子相干性联系起来：*"These results reveal a spin-charge-intertwined ground state and establish the microscopic foundation for the exceptional coherence of the magnetic exciton in NiPS₃."* 该结论在领域中的意义是为 NiPS₃ 磁激子模型提供局域电子结构约束。

    ---

    Main text / Introduction

    Entanglement provides the conceptual frame

    研究把 NiPS₃ 的问题放入更广泛的量子纠缠语境。开头强调：*"Entanglement lies at the heart of quantum mechanics."* 随后指出实验验证纠缠态长期困难，甚至与 EPR 悖论的历史争论相连：*"its understanding and experimental verification remain profoundly challenging, as exemplified by the long-standing debate surrounding the Einstein-Podolsky-Rosen paradox."* 这说明 NiPS₃ 的意义不只是材料特性，而是固体中可观测多体纠缠态的识别。

    Zhang-Rice state is a canonical correlated-electron entangled state

    Zhang-Rice 态被定位为关联电子系统中自旋单态 / 三重态纠缠的现代实现。原文指出：*"In correlated electron systems, a modern realization of such entanglement is the Zhang-Rice state, originally proposed to describe the emergent many-body physics of high-temperature copper-oxide superconductors."* 在铜氧化物中经典 Zhang-Rice singlet 是 Cu 3d 空穴与 O 2p 配体空穴形成的局域复合态；在 NiPS₃ 中对应的是 Zhang-Rice triplet。

    NiPS₃ has a monoclinic honeycomb crystal structure

    材料结构信息明确：NiPS₃ 是单斜晶体，空间群 C2/m，Ni²⁺ 离子形成蜂窝晶格。原文为：*"It has a monoclinic crystal structure with a space group C2/m with the Ni²⁺ ions arranged in a honeycomb lattice."* 蜂窝几何和层状范德华结构为 zigzag 磁序和三态向列性提供晶格基础。

    Zigzag antiferromagnetic order occurs below 155 K

    NiPS₃ 的磁基态是 zigzag 反铁磁序，Néel 温度 Tₙ = 155 K。原文写道：*"It undergoes a zigzag magnetic ordering below the Néel temperature Tₙ = 155 K, which breaks the three-fold rotational symmetry."* 破缺三重旋转对称性意味着磁序天然关联到晶格 / 电子向列自由度。

    Magnetic exciton shows exceptional coherence at low temperature

    NiPS₃ 最突出的实验现象是磁有序相中的激子线宽急剧变窄，并在低温达到仪器分辨率极限。关键数值是 低于 50 K 时线宽约 0.4 meV：*"becomes resolution-limited at low temperatures, achieving an unprecedented linewidth of approximately 0.4 meV below 50 K."* 这种极窄线宽远超常规局域 d-d 激发或普通激子的预期。

    Thickness dependence links the exciton to magnetism

    磁激子随厚度降低显著展宽，在单层中完全消失。原文指出：*"it broadens significantly when the thickness is reduced to below three layers and disappears entirely in the monolayer limit."* 这排除了纯局域晶场激发解释，强调激子与长程 / 准长程磁关联耦合：*"underscoring intimate coupling between magnetism and the exciton."*

    Multiple competing exciton models lack a unified microscopic picture

    NiPS₃ 磁激子的解释模型很多，包括 Zhang-Rice exciton、triplet-singlet exciton、Hund’s exciton、polaron exciton、spin-entangled exciton。原文列举：*"a Zhang-Rice exciton, a triplet-singlet exciton, a Hund’s exciton, a polaron exciton, and a spin-entangled exciton."* 但这些模型只解释部分现象，缺乏统一微观图像：*"a coherent, unified microscopic picture has remained elusive."*

    The unresolved issue is the nature of the entangled ground state

    关键科学问题不是仅确定激子峰，而是确定激子背后的基态电子构型。原文强调：*"definitive experimental evidence identifying the nature of the underlying quantum-entangled ground state has been lacking, leaving the origin of the exceptional exciton coherence unresolved."* 因而需要能直接探测配体位点与 Ni 位点耦合的实验手段。

    ³³S NMR in the paramagnetic state targets the local charge-transfer configuration

    研究策略是在顺磁相中进行 ³³S NMR，避免磁有序相复杂展宽，同时探测局域电子结构。原文写道：*"we present a ³³S nuclear magnetic resonance (NMR) study of ³³S-enriched NiPS₃ single crystals in the paramagnetic (PM) state."* 顺磁相仍保留局域 ZRT 构型，因此可从 Knight shift 与四极参数判断配体空穴。

    Angle- and temperature-dependent spectra reveal transferred spin density and p-d hybridization

    ³³S 谱的温度与角度依赖揭示 S 3p 转移自旋密度和 Ni 3d 强杂化。原文概括为：*"Detailed analysis of temperature- and angle-dependent, quadrupole-perturbed ³³S spectra reveals substantial transferred spin density on the S 3p orbitals and strong hybridization with Ni 3d moments."* 这些被定义为 self-doped Zhang-Rice triplet ground state 的标志：*"both hallmarks of a self-doped Zhang-Rice triplet ground state."*

    ³³S and ³¹P relaxation contrast isolates nematic charge fluctuations

    ³³S 的 T₁⁻¹ 接近 Tₙ 幂律发散，而 ³¹P 不发散。原文指出：*"A striking observation is the power-law divergence of the ³³S nuclear spin-lattice relaxation rate T₁⁻¹ approaching Tₙ. Remarkably, this divergent behavior is absent in the ³¹P relaxation data."* 二者对比说明 ³³S 探测到的不是普通 Ni 自旋临界涨落，而是与 Ni 磁矩向列相关的电荷 / EFG 涨落：*"the fluctuations probed by ³³S originate from nematic correlations of the Ni moments."*

    ---

    Experimental details / Methods

    ³³S-enriched single crystals were grown by chemical vapor transport

    单晶制备采用 chemical vapor transport（CVT）。原文给出：*"Single crystals of NiPS₃ enriched with ³³S were synthesized using the chemical vapor transport (CVT) method."* ³³S 富集非常关键，因为天然丰度低会导致 ³³S NMR 灵敏度不足。

    Starting materials and sulfur excess were precisely specified

    原料包括 Ni powders（Alfa Aesar, 99.99%）、P powder（Sigma-Aldrich, 99.99%）和 ³³S（Sigma-Aldrich, 99%），并加入 10 wt% excess ³³S。原文为：*"Stoichiometric amounts of Ni powders (Alfa Aesar, 99.99%), P powder (Sigma-Aldrich, 99.99%) and ³³S (Sigma-Aldrich, 99%) were mixed, with an additional 10 wt % excess of ³³S."*

    Oxidation was suppressed by Ar glovebox handling

    所有起始材料在氩气手套箱中处理和混合，以避免氧化。原文写道：*"All starting materials were handled and mixed in an Ar-filled glovebox to prevent oxidation."* 对硫磷化合物而言，氧化会改变化学计量与局域 EFG，影响 NMR 解释。

    Growth conditions were 750°C / 720°C for 7 days

    混合物被封入抽真空石英安瓿，在双温区炉中生长 7 天，热端 750°C，冷端 720°C。原文细节为：*"The mixture was sealed in an evacuated quartz ampoule and placed in a two-zone furnace for 7 days, the hot and cold zones maintained at 750°C and 720°C, respectively."*

    Composition and structure were checked by EDX and XRD

    晶体化学组成通过 EDX 验证，结构通过 XRD 确认。原文为：*"The chemical composition of the grown crystals was confirmed by energy-dispersive X-ray spectroscopy"*；结构方面：*"The crystal structure was confirmed through XRD measurements using a commercial diffractometer (Rigaku Miniflex II)."*

    ³³S enrichment did not alter bulk magnetic susceptibility

    富集样品与未富集样品体磁化率一致。原文指出：*"we verified that the bulk magnetic susceptibility of the ³³S-enriched crystal is identical to that of the unenriched one."* 这排除了同位素富集或合成差异导致磁性改变的可能性。

    NMR conditions were field 5.93 T and temperature 150–320 K

    ³³S NMR 在 3 × 2 × 0.2 mm³ 单晶上进行，外场 5.93 T，温度 150–320 K。原文为：*"³³S (nuclear spin I = 3/2) NMR was carried out in a ³³S enriched NiPS₃ single crystal (3 × 2 × 0.2 mm³) at an external field of 5.93 T and in the range of temperature 150—320 K."*

    Angular alignment used a goniometer

    样品通过测角仪旋转，以精确控制外场方向。原文为：*"The sample was rotated using a goniometer for the exact alignment along the external field."* 角度依赖谱线对于确定 EFG 主轴方向至关重要。

    Spectra were acquired by spin echo with 2–3 μs π/2 pulses

    ³³S 谱采用标准 spin-echo 技术，典型 π/2 pulse length = 2–3 μs。原文为：*"The ³³S NMR spectra were acquired by a standard spin-echo technique with a typical π/2 pulse length 2–3 μs."*

    T₁ recovery function accounts for I = 3/2 central transition relaxation

    ³³S 核自旋-晶格弛豫率通过饱和脉冲后磁化恢复拟合获得，函数为

    1 − M(t)/M(∞) = A[0.1 exp(−t/T₁) + 0.9 exp(−6t/T₁)]。原文给出：*"The ³³S nuclear spin-lattice relaxation rate T₁⁻¹ was obtained by fitting the recovery of the nuclear magnetization M(t) after a saturating pulse to the following fitting function..."* 其中 A 理想为 1：*"where A is a fitting parameter that is ideally unity."*

    Measurements were restricted to the paramagnetic state

    Tₙ 以下信号因强磁性展宽消失，因此 NMR 只在顺磁相进行。原文说明：*"NMR measurements were performed exclusively in the PM state, because the signal is lost below Tₙ due to substantial magnetic broadening."* 这是解释范围的重要边界：所有 ZRT 证据来自局域构型在顺磁相中的表现。

    ---

    Figure 1 and ³³S quadrupole spectra

    ³³S central transition was observed for H ∥ c*

    在外场 H = 5.93 T 且 H ⟂ ab / H ∥ c* 条件下，观察到 ³³S 中心跃迁 1/2 ↔ −1/2。原文为：*"The ³³S NMR central transition (1/2 ↔ −1/2) was found in ³³S-enriched NiPS₃ single crystals at an external field H = 5.93 T applied perpendicular to the ab plane."*

    The 180 K spectrum contains two sharp lines and one broad feature

    180 K 代表谱由两个尖锐峰和一个宽特征组成。原文描述：*"Figure 1(b) shows a representative ³³S spectrum measured at 180 K, consisting of two sharp lines and one broad feature."* 这说明即使在 H ∥ c* 下，局域环境仍存在细微不等价或残余分裂。

    Angular rotation rapidly broadens the spectrum

    当 c* 与外场夹角 θ 增大，谱线迅速展宽并变复杂。原文写道：*"As the angle θ between the c* axis and H increases, the spectrum broadens rapidly and evolves into a complicated structure."* 对 θ ≳ 15°，单线追踪变得极难：*"For θ ≳ 15°, tracing the angular evolution of individual lines becomes exceedingly difficult."*

    H ∥ ab produces three groups of resonance lines

    在 θ = 90°，H ∥ ab 条件下，出现三组 ³³S 共振线，每组含 2–4 个组分。原文为：*"we therefore aligned the ab plane parallel to H (θ = 90°) and obtained three distinct groups of ³³S resonance lines, each containing 2–4 components."* 三组线对应三种 EFG 主轴方向相对外场的取向。

    Second-order quadrupole shift is essential for I = 3/2 ³³S

    ³³S 的核自旋 I = 3/2 且具有显著四极矩，因此中心跃迁存在二阶四极位移 Δν₂nd。原文为：*"Because ³³S has nuclear spin I = 3/2 and sizable quadrupole moment Q, the central transition experiences a second-order quadrupole shift Δν₂nd in the presence of an electric field gradient (EFG)."* 这使 ³³S 谱不仅反映磁超精细场，也反映局域电荷环境。

    Initial symmetry expectation placed Vzz tilted out of the ab plane by around 30°

    基于局域位点对称性，最初预期 S 位点 EFG 主轴 Vzz 垂直于 NiS₆ 八面体边，并相对 ab 面倾斜约 30°。原文为：*"the principal component Vzz of the local EFG tensor at the S nuclei is expected to point perpendicular to the NiS₆ octahedral edges, tilting out of the ab plane by ∼30°."*

    Three-fold lattice symmetry explains the three line groups for H ∥ ab

    三重晶格对称性及四极相互作用可定性解释 H ∥ ab 下的三组共振线。原文指出：*"the three-fold lattice symmetry and associated quadrupole interactions qualitatively account for the three distinct resonance groups observed for H ∥ ab."* 原因是三类 S 位点的 Vzz 与 H 夹角不同：*"since the angle between Vzz and the external field differs among the three ³³S sites."*

    H ∥ c* collapses the three local spectra

    对 H ∥ c*，三个 ³³S 位点的局域对称性给出相同谱线，因此谱线几乎重合。原文为：*"For H ∥ c*, by contrast, the local symmetries of the three ³³S sites yield the identical resonant spectrum, thereby explaining the nearly collapsed spectral lines."* 残余分裂可能来自轻微错位或 S(1)/S(2) EFG 大小差异：*"The residual line splitting may arise from a slight sample misalignment and/or small differences in EFG magnitude between the S(1) and S(2) sites."*

    Detailed angular analysis places Vzz within the ab plane

    精细角度分析推翻了初始倾斜预期，显示 Vzz 实际位于 ab 面内。原文直接写道：*"A detailed analysis of the angle dependence of the ³³S lines reveals that the Vzz components actually lie within the ab plane."* 这提示局域电荷分布具有强烈面内各向异性。

    Quadrupole parameters are νQ = 6.4 MHz and η = 0.1

    角度依赖谱可由 νQ = 6.4 MHz 与 η = 0.1 拟合，且三重 Vzz 取向限制在 ab 面内。原文为：*"the angle dependence of the ³³S spectrum is well reproduced by a quadrupole frequency νQ = 6.4 MHz and an anisotropy parameter η = 0.1, with the three-fold Vzz orientations confined within the ab plane."*

    The large νQ signals strong S 3p–Ni 3d hybridization

    νQ = 6.4 MHz 显著大于层状过渡金属二硫化物典型值，并接近分子 ²Π SH 系统。原文指出：*"The extracted νQ = 6.4 MHz substantially exceeds values typical of layered transition-metal disulfides and is comparable to that of the molecular ²Π SH system."* 这种异常四极相互作用难以用纯局域 Ni²⁺ d⁸ 图像解释：*"hardly understood within a purely localized d⁸ description of the Ni²⁺ ions."* 更合理解释是 S 3p 空穴与非对称 Ni 3d 轨道强杂化：*"suggesting strong hybridization of the S 3p holes with asymmetrically arranged surrounding Ni 3d orbitals."*

    ---

    Figure 2 and Knight shift evidence for ZRT

    Temperature-dependent ³³S spectra preserve their shape up to room temperature

    在 H ∥ c* 条件下测量温度依赖 ³³S 谱，除接近 Tₙ 时信号强度快速下降外，谱形直到室温基本不变。原文为：*"Apart from the rapid suppression of signal intensity near Tₙ, attributable to the wipeout effect caused by the shortening of NMR relaxation times, the overall spectral shape remains essentially unchanged up to room temperature."* 这说明局域电子结构在顺磁相中稳定。

    Peaks A and B enable reliable ³³S Knight shift extraction

    两个尖峰 A 和 B 在整个温区保持存在，允许提取 ³³S Knight shift。原文为：*"the sharp peaks labelled A and B persist over the whole temperature range, enabling reliable determination of the ³³S Knight shift."* Knight shift 定义为

    K = (ν − ν₀)/ν₀ × 100%，其中 ν 已扣除二阶四极位移。原文为：*"K is defined as (ν − ν₀)/ν₀ × 100% where ν₀ is the unshifted Larmor frequency and ν is the resonance frequency corrected for the second-order quadrupole shift."*

    ³³S and ³¹P Knight shifts follow the same susceptibility

    ³³S Knight shift 与 ³¹P Knight shift 温度依赖相似，并在约 250 K 附近有宽峰，与体磁化率一致。原文为：*"The temperature dependence of ³³K resembles that of the ³¹P Knight shift ³¹K, with both exhibiting a broad maximum near 250 K, which is consistent with bulk susceptibility."* 这证明两种核都探测到与 Ni 磁矩相关的同一局域自旋磁化率：*"This demonstrates that both ³³S and ³¹P nuclei probe the same local spin susceptibility associated with the Ni moments."*

    K–χ analysis gives a huge positive ³³S hyperfine coupling

    Knight shift 自旋部分满足 Kspin = Ahf χspin。原文写道：*"The spin part of the Knight shift is proportional to the local spin susceptibility, Kspin = Ahfχspin."* 通过 K–χ 图，低于 250 K 线性拟合得到 ³³Ahf = 44.2 kOe/μB。原文为：*"A linear fit below 250 K yields ³³Ahf = 44.2 kOe/μB."*

    ³¹P hyperfine coupling is small and negative

    ³¹P 对应超精细耦合为 ³¹Ahf = −1.8 kOe/μB。原文为：*"For ³¹P, the corresponding value is ³¹Ahf = −1.8 kOe/μB."* 二者数量级差异约 25 倍，说明 ³³S 不是简单通过远程偶极场感受 Ni 磁矩。

    Linearity breaks down above 250 K for both nuclei

    两种核在 250 K 以上的 K–χ 线性关系均失效。原文指出：*"The breakdown of linearity above 250 K for both nuclei further supports their common origin in the Ni spin susceptibility."* 这暗示高温区可能存在额外温度依赖项、短程关联变化或轨道贡献变化，但共同失效支持同一 Ni 自旋来源。

    Large ³³S Ahf implies anomalously high S 3p spin density

    计算显示若仅来自 Ni 磁矩，³³S 的 Ahf 应很小并接近 ³¹P，因此实验中巨大 ³³S Ahf 只能来自 S 3p 轨道上的显著自旋密度。原文为：*"the much larger hyperfine coupling at ³³S than that at ³¹P implies unusually high spin density on the otherwise completely filled S 3p orbitals."* 结论是 ³³S Knight shift 主要探测从 Ni 3d 转移而来的 S 3p moments / holes：*"³³K primarily probes S 3p moments (holes) transferred from Ni 3d orbitals."*

    S 3p and Ni 3d moments form a unified spin system

    ³¹P 主要通过偶极耦合反映 Ni 3d 磁矩，而 ³³S 反映 S 3p 空穴；二者温度依赖一致说明两类矩强耦合。原文为：*"the identical temperature dependence of both ³¹K and ³³K demonstrates that the S 3p and Ni 3d moments are strongly coupled, acting as components of a unified spin system."*

    The charge-transfer state preserves Ni²⁺ ³A₂ spin-triplet symmetry

    结果支持 Ni²⁺ d⁸ 的 ³A₂ 自旋三重态对称性在 d⁹L̲ 电荷转移态中保留。原文写道：*"These results suggest that the spin-triplet ³A₂ symmetry of Ni²⁺ (d⁸) ions is preserved in the charge-transfer state with d⁹L̲ configuration, where L̲ denotes a ligand hole."* 这里 L̲ 表示配体空穴。

    Ground state is a p-d hybridized Zhang-Rice triplet

    NiPS₃ 基态被描述为 d⁸ 与 d⁹L̲ 构型叠加，即 p-d 杂化自旋三重态 / Zhang-Rice triplet。原文为：*"The ground state of NiPS₃ is therefore best described as a p-d hybridized spin-triplet state, characterized by the superposition of d⁸ and d⁹L̲ configurations, namely a Zhang-Rice triplet (ZRT) state."* 这与“dominant d⁸ character”的局域模型相对立：*"rather than a state with dominant d⁸ character."*

    Hund’s exciton scenario already requires substantial ligand-hole admixture

    即便是以 d⁸ 为主的 Hund’s exciton 图像，也估计约 40% d⁹L̲ ligand-hole admixture。原文为：*"Even within the Hund’s exciton scenario, which primarily focuses on a d⁸-based description, a substantial d⁹L̲ ligand-hole admixture of approximately 40% was estimated."* 这说明配体空穴成分并非边缘修正，而是定量显著。

    ZRT is valid in both PM and AFM phases as a local configuration

    ZRT 被视为局域电子构型，因此顺磁相与反铁磁相均适用；AFM 相只是这些局域三重态的长程排列。原文为：*"since the ZRT represents the local electronic configuration of NiPS₃, it remains a valid description in both the PM and AFM phases, with the latter corresponding to the long-range alignment of these local triplet many-body states."*

    Localized d⁸-based exciton scenarios conflict with the NMR results

    基于局域 d⁸ 的替代模型与 NMR 证据不兼容。原文表述很强：*"Consequently, all alternative exciton scenarios, which are essentially based on the localized d⁸ configuration, are incompatible with these NMR results."* 这里的排除逻辑来自 ³³S Ahf、νQ 和共同 Knight shift 温度依赖。

    Residual NMR shift reaches an unprecedented 10.7%

    K–χ 图显示巨大残余位移 10.7%。原文为：*"An unexpected finding in Fig. 2(c) is the unprecedentedly large residual NMR shift of 10.7%."* 其中约 2% 来自 νQ = 6.4 MHz 的二阶四极贡献，剩余 8.7% 应归因于轨道 Knight shift：*"This shift includes the second-order quadrupole contribution, approximately 2% for νQ = 6.4 MHz, implying that the additional 8.7% shift ought to be attributed to the orbital Knight shift."*

    Orbital Knight shift implies χVV ≈ 0.8 × 10⁻³ emu/mol

    轨道 Knight shift 与 Van Vleck 磁化率关系为

    Korb = 2⟨r⁻³⟩/NA χVV。原文为：*"Korb is related to the Van Vleck susceptibility χVV via Korb = 2⟨r⁻³⟩/NAχVV."* 使用 ⟨r⁻³⟩3p = 4.8 a.u.，得到 χVV ≈ 0.8 × 10⁻³ emu/mol：*"Using ⟨r⁻³⟩3p = 4.8 a.u. for a 3p orbital, we obtain χVV ≈ 0.8 × 10⁻³ emu/mol."*

    Local crystal-field model cannot explain the large orbital shift

    Ni²⁺ 在八面体晶场中有 ³A₂ 轨道单态基态和 ³T₂ 轨道三重第一激发态，二者混合可产生轨道磁化率。原文为：*"In an octahedral crystal field, Ni²⁺ ions possess a ³A₂ orbital-singlet ground state and a ³T₂ orbital-triplet first-excited state."* 但所需激发能隙要比计算值 1 eV 小一个数量级：*"the estimated χVV requires the excitation gap Δ to be an order of magnitude smaller than the calculated value of 1 eV."*

    Inter-site orbital currents may contribute to the large orbital Knight shift

    大轨道位移提示超出标准局域晶场模型的贡献，可能来自 ZRT 中固有的跨位点轨道电流。原文为：*"The large orbital Knight shift thus suggests contributions beyond the standard local crystal-field model, possibly arising from the significant inter-site orbital currents inherent to the hybridized ZRT state."* 这进一步强化了非局域 p-d 杂化图像。

    ---

    Figure 3 and relaxation dynamics

    ³³S T₁⁻¹ increases toward Tₙ whereas ³¹P T₁⁻¹ decreases

    低能动力学通过 ³³S T₁⁻¹ 探测，并与同场向 ³¹P 数据比较。原文为：*"Having established the ZRT ground state in the PM phase of NiPS₃, we now turn to the low-energy spin/charge dynamics probed by the ³³S nuclear spin-lattice relaxation rate."* 结果呈强烈对比：*"Upon cooling, ³³T₁⁻¹ increases, exhibiting a divergent behavior as Tₙ is approached, in sharp contrast to the monotonic decrease observed for ³¹T₁⁻¹."*

    ³¹P decrease indicates absence of collective spin fluctuations above Tₙ

    ³¹P 弛豫率单调下降意味着 Tₙ 以上没有普通集体自旋临界涨落。原文明确：*"which indicates the absence of collective spin fluctuations above Tₙ."* 如果接近反铁磁临界点存在强自旋慢化，³¹P 理应增强，除非被几何过滤完全消除。

    Geometric filtering at P is ruled out

    可能解释之一是 P 位点超精细形式因子 A(q) 在相关 q 处为零，导致看不到 AFM 涨落。原文提出并排除：*"The contrasting relaxation behavior may result from geometric filtering, if the hyperfine form factor A(q) vanishes at the P site."* 计算显示 A(q) 对所有相关 q 保持有限：*"our calculations show that A(q) remains finite for all relevant q, ruling out a symmetry-imposed cancellation of AFM fluctuations."*

    ³³S divergence must arise from EFG fluctuations

    由于普通自旋涨落和几何过滤被排除，³³S 发散必须来自 EFG fluctuations，即电场梯度涨落。原文为：*"Consequently, the divergence in ³³T₁⁻¹ must stem from fluctuations of the EFG, which couple to quadrupolar ³³S (I = 3/2), but not to ³¹P (I = 1/2)."* 这是区分电荷动力学与自旋动力学的关键。

    EFG fluctuations are linked to Ni 3d–S 3p charge transfer

    NiPS₃ 中 EFG 涨落自然来自 Ni 3d 与 S 3p 之间的电荷转移动力学。原文为：*"In NiPS₃, such EFG fluctuations are naturally linked to charge dynamics involving Ni 3d and S 3p charge transfer."* 这把 ³³S T₁⁻¹ 发散与 ZRT 的配体空穴自由度连接起来。

    χT scaling explains the spin part of relaxation

    ³¹P T₁⁻¹ 随温度降低的抑制跟随 χT，说明顺磁相中静态短程 AFM 关联主导自旋弛豫贡献。原文为：*"the suppression of ³¹T₁⁻¹ with decreasing temperature follows the temperature dependence of χT, suggesting that static short-range AFM correlations dominate the spin contribution to T₁⁻¹ in the PM phase."*

    Reduced relaxation rate isolates dynamic spin correlations

    定义归一化弛豫率

    R₁ ≡ (T₁χT)⁻¹，用于剥离静态磁化率和热因子。原文为：*"To isolate the contribution of dynamic spin correlations, we define the reduced spin-lattice relaxation rate R₁ ≡ (T₁χT)⁻¹."* 这是一种类似临界动力学分析的缩放处理。

    ³¹R₁ is nearly temperature independent down to Tₙ

    归一化后，³¹P 的 R₁ 几乎不随温度变化，确认没有临界自旋动力学。原文为：*"This correction yields an almost temperature-independent ³¹R₁ down to Tₙ, confirming the absence of critical spin dynamics."*

    ³³R₁ follows a power-law divergence with exponent 0.464

    ³³S 的 R₁ 在冷却时快速增加，并满足幂律：

    ³³R₁ ∝ |T − T₀|⁻⁰·⁴⁶⁴。原文为：*"In striking contrast, ³³R₁ increases rapidly on cooling and follows a power-law divergence, ³³R₁ ∝ |T − T₀|⁻⁰·⁴⁶⁴."* 拟合得到 T₀ = 152 K，接近 Tₙ = 155 K：*"The fitting of the data yields the characterization temperature T₀ = 152 K, which is remarkably close to Tₙ = 155 K."*

    ---

    Unified interpretation and discussion

    Knight shift and quadrupole results form a consistent ZRT picture

    ³³S 与 ³¹P Knight shift 表明 S 3p 轨道上存在显著转移自旋密度，并与 Ni 3d 磁矩强耦合；这与顺磁相 self-doped ZRT 基态一致。原文总结：*"The ³³S and ³¹P Knight shift measurements demonstrate substantial transferred spin density on S 3p orbitals and its strong coupling with Ni 3d moments, consistent with the formation of a self-doped ZRT ground state in the PM phase."*

    Large νQ is naturally explained by strong p-d hybridization

    异常大的 νQ = 6.4 MHz 被解释为 ZRT 固有的强 p-d 杂化造成的局域电荷不对称。原文为：*"The pronounced p-d hybridization intrinsic to the ZRT state naturally explains the unusually large quadrupole frequency νQ = 6.4 MHz observed in our measurements."*

    Low-energy spin dynamics is inactive despite spin-triplet character

    尽管 ZRT 具有强自旋三重态特征，核弛豫中低能自旋动力学并不活跃。原文指出：*"Surprisingly, despite the dominant spin character of the ZRT state, the low-energy spin dynamics is effectively inactive in the nuclear spin-lattice relaxation rate measurements."* 这是全文最反直觉的发现之一。

    ³³S relaxation divergence indicates charge-dominated ordering instability

    ³³S 弛豫率发散指向主要涉及电荷涨落的长程有序不稳定性，且不同于 zigzag AFM 序。原文为：*"the ³³S relaxation rate exhibits a power-law divergence toward Tₙ, suggesting a long-range ordering instability that predominantly involves charge fluctuations, which is distinct from the zig-zag AFM ordering."*

    Biquadratic spin interactions may enhance quantum fluctuations

    自旋与电荷涨落谱的差异可能源于双二次自旋相互作用增强的量子涨落。原文为：*"The contrasting behaviors of spin and charge fluctuation spectra may originate from quantum fluctuations enhanced by biquadratic spin interactions."* biquadratic interaction 通常形如 (Si·Sj)²，能增强自旋向列关联。

    Ligand hole density depends on relative Ni spin alignment

    ZRT 中强自旋-电荷耦合意味着桥接两个 Ni 的 S 位点空穴密度取决于两侧 Ni 自旋相对取向。原文写道：*"the hole density on a given S site bridging two Ni sites is dependent on the relative spin arrangement."* 具体地，铁磁耦合时空穴密度略高于反铁磁耦合：*"it is slightly higher for ferromagnetic than for antiferromagnetic coupling, due to the Hund’s coupling on the ligand orbitals."*

    Charge density couples to spin bilinears

    S 桥位配体空穴密度可写为

    n̄ij = n̄0 + n̄1(Si · Sj)。原文为：*"The corresponding coupling can be expressed as n̄ij = n̄0 + n̄1(Si · Sj), where n̄0 and n̄1 denote the spin-independent and spin-dependent contributions of the self-doped S holes, respectively."* 这说明电荷涨落不是独立电荷序，而是由自旋双线性控制的复合自由度。

    Charge fluctuation correlations are governed by nematic correlations

    电荷关联函数

    C n̄ij,n̄kl = ⟨n̄ij n̄kl⟩ − ⟨n̄ij⟩⟨n̄kl⟩

    可转化为自旋双线性关联：

    n̄1²[⟨(Si·Sj)(Sk·Sl)⟩ − ⟨Si·Sj⟩⟨Sk·Sl⟩]。原文为：*"The correlation function of charge fluctuations ... is therefore governed by the nematic correlations of Ni moments."* 这里的 nematic correlations 指键能 / 自旋点积在不同晶格方向上的各向异性相关。

    ³³R₁ divergence is interpreted as critical nematic fluctuations

    ³³S 归一化弛豫率发散被解释为与电荷自由度耦合的临界向列涨落。原文为：*"the observed divergence of ³³R₁ can be interpreted as a manifestation of critical nematic fluctuations that couple to the charge degrees of freedom through spin-orbit entanglement."* 这里 spin-orbit entanglement 更准确地说是自旋、轨道和配体电荷在 ZRT 中不可分离。

    Bulk nematic order has not yet been observed

    体材料中尚未观测到明确向列长程序。原文承认：*"Although no experimental signature of nematic order has yet been observed in bulk material."* 这是解释链条中的实验限制。

    Single-layer NiPS₃ shows vestigial nematicity

    单层极限中已有 vestigial nematic phase 报道，因强量子涨落抑制长程 AFM 序。原文为：*"a vestigial nematic phase has been reported in the single-layer limit, where strong quantum fluctuations suppress the long-range AFM order."* 这为体材料中 Tₙ 以上的层内向列涨落提供类比基础。

    Quasi-2D thermal fluctuations can preserve intralayer nematic correlations above Tₙ

    在体 NiPS₃ 中，准二维层状晶格的热涨落可能破坏真正长程序，但允许单层内向列不稳定性持续存在。原文为：*"thermal fluctuations in the quasi-two-dimensional lattice may destroy long-range spin and nematic order while allowing a nematic instability to persist within individual layers."* 因层间解耦，真实长程序难建立，但层内向列关联仍强：*"interlayer decoupling prevents the establishment of true long-range order, but robust intralayer nematic correlations survive above Tₙ."*

    NMR is uniquely sensitive to fluctuating 2D nematicity

    中子散射等体探针对二维涨落不敏感，而 NMR 作为实空间局域探针可检测这类涨落。原文为：*"While bulk probes like neutron scattering barely detect 2D fluctuations, NMR, as a local probe in real space, is uniquely sensitive to such fluctuating 2D nematicity."* 但该向列不稳定性被 Tₙ 处磁转变抢先截断：*"this nematic instability is preempted by the magnetic transition at Tₙ."*

    Nematicity-driven magnetic ordering is proposed

    当层间向列相关足够强时，增强的自旋-电荷耦合可能沿向列方向驱动自旋排列，从而在 Tₙ 稳定 zigzag AFM。原文为：*"once the interlayer nematic correlations become sufficiently strong, the enhanced spin-charge coupling drives the spin alignment along the nematic orientation, thereby stabilizing the zigzag AFM order at Tₙ."*

    This scenario explains first-order AFM transition and ordered-moment tilt

    向列驱动磁序情景可解释 ³¹P NMR 发现的一级 AFM 转变，以及有序磁矩朝 S(1) 的异常倾斜。原文为：*"Such a nematicity-driven magnetic ordering scenario naturally accounts for both the first-order AFM transition revealed by our ³¹P NMR study and the unusual tilt of the ordered moments toward S(1)."*

    Related FePSe₃ results suggest generality in vdW antiferromagnets

    同构 FePSe₃ 在单轴应变下的 AFM 相中出现向列性，支持向列序与磁序紧密关联。原文为：*"The recent observation of nematicity within the AFM phase of isostructural FePSe₃ under uniaxial strain further supports the intimate link between nematic and magnetic orders."* 这提示该机制可能是范德华反铁磁体的一般特征：*"suggesting that this interplay may be a general feature of van der Waals antiferromagnets."*

    研究资助来源包括 Samsung Science & Technology Foundation 与韩国 NRF Leading Researcher Program。原文为：*"The work at SNU was supported by the Samsung Science & Technology Foundation (Grant No. SSTFBA2101-05) and the Leading Researcher Program of the National Research Foundation of Korea (Grant No. RS-2020-NR049405)."*
