    Data Availability

    Data are available upon reasonable request

    数据可在合理请求下获得。原文为：*"The data that supports the findings of this article are available upon reasonable request from the authors."*

    ---

    第四部分：深度理解与语言支持（Understanding & Nuance）

    1. 术语解析

    Zhang-Rice triplet（ZRT）

    Zhang-Rice 态原本来自铜氧化物：Cu 3d 空穴与 O 2p 配体空穴形成局域复合态。铜氧化物中通常是 singlet；NiPS₃ 中由于 Ni²⁺ d⁸ 本身为 S = 1，配体空穴与 Ni 3d 空穴形成的是 triplet。文中关键表达是 *"a p-d hybridized spin-triplet state, characterized by the superposition of d⁸ and d⁹L̲ configurations"*。微妙点在于：ZRT 不是单粒子激发，而是局域多体基态构型。

    Self-doped hole

    Self-doped 不等于外部化学掺杂，而是由于电荷转移能、p-d 杂化和共价性，配体轨道天然带有空穴成分。文中表达为 *"a self-doped hole in the S 3p orbitals"*。其物理含义是名义价态 Ni²⁺ / S²⁻ 图像不完整，真实波函数含有 d⁹L̲ 成分。

    Knight shift

    Knight shift 是核磁共振频率相对裸 Larmor 频率的位移，反映局域电子自旋 / 轨道磁化率。文中定义为 *"K is defined as (ν − ν₀)/ν₀ × 100%"*。³³S Knight shift 巨大说明硫位点不是磁性旁观者，而承载实际自旋密度。

    Electric field gradient（EFG）

    EFG 是核位置处电势二阶导数张量，反映周围电荷分布的不均匀性。³³S 因 I = 3/2 有四极矩，可通过 EFG 感受局域电荷环境。文中 *"fluctuations of the EFG"* 实际对应配体电荷转移和局域电荷各向异性涨落。

    Vestigial nematicity

    Vestigial 指“残余的、从更高阶序中遗留下来的”。在磁系统中，即使长程 AFM 序被涨落破坏，仍可能保留破缺旋转对称性的向列序。文中 *"vestigial nematic phase"* 指单层 NiPS₃ 中无长程反铁磁序但仍有三态向列性。

    ---

    2. 疑难查证

    为什么 ³³S 能看到发散而 ³¹P 看不到？

    ³³S 与 ³¹P 的关键差异不是位置不同这么简单，而是核自旋不同。³³S 有 I = 3/2，具有核四极矩，因此能耦合到 EFG 涨落；³¹P 是 I = 1/2，没有四极矩，主要通过磁性超精细场感受自旋涨落。若 Tₙ 上方存在普通临界自旋涨落，³¹P 也应看到增强；但 ³¹P 的归一化 R₁ 几乎常数。因此 ³³S 的发散更合理地来自电荷 / EFG 涨落。

    为什么电荷涨落可以叫“向列涨落”？

    S 位点空穴密度与两侧 Ni 自旋点积相关：

    n̄ij = n̄0 + n̄1(Si·Sj)。

    如果不同 Ni–Ni 键方向上的 Si·Sj 相关增强或变得不等价，就会造成不同方向上的 S 空穴密度不同。这种不一定产生净磁矩，却会破坏三重旋转对称性的涨落，就是自旋向列涨落。³³S 看到的是电荷密度 / EFG 的临界慢化，但其根源是 Ni 自旋双线性相关的临界增强。

    为什么 ZRT 能解释磁激子的长寿命？

    局域 d⁸ 晶场激发通常会强烈耦合声子、晶格畸变或多种衰减通道，不容易形成极窄线宽。ZRT 中激子建立在强 p-d 杂化和自旋三重态约束上，电荷与自旋自由度不是分离的；磁有序相中长程自旋排列可保护或选择特定激发通道，使激子线宽在低温达到分辨率极限。NMR 结果提供的是基态微观前提：S 3p 空穴与 Ni 3d 磁矩确实构成统一多体态。

    为什么说局域 d⁸ 模型不够？

    如果 NiPS₃ 是纯 Ni²⁺ d⁸，硫 3p 轨道应近似满占据，³³S 上自旋密度很小，³³S Ahf 应接近由 Ni 磁矩偶极场产生的小值。然而实验得到 ³³Ahf = 44.2 kOe/μB，远大于 ³¹Ahf = −1.8 kOe/μB；同时 νQ = 6.4 MHz 也异常大。二者共同要求硫 3p 上存在显著空穴和强 p-d 杂化。

    ---

    第五部分：创新评估与关联（Synthesis & Novelty）

    1. 创新性判断

    从光学 / RIXS 争论推进到局域核磁证据

    过去 2–5 年 NiPS₃ 研究主要围绕磁激子的光谱特征、厚度依赖、偏振各向异性、RIXS 激发色散和理论模型竞争展开。Zhang-Rice exciton、Hund’s exciton、triplet-singlet exciton、polaron exciton、spin-entangled exciton 都可解释部分观测，但缺乏直接识别基态配体空穴的局域证据。³³S NMR 直接探测硫位点，把问题从“激子峰如何拟合”推进到“基态波函数是否含 d⁹L̲”。

    首次把 ³³S 位点作为配体空穴探针用于 NiPS₃ 的 ZRT 判定

    ³³S 富集单晶 NMR 技术难度高，但对 S 3p 轨道极其敏感。通过 νQ = 6.4 MHz、η = 0.1、³³Ahf = 44.2 kOe/μB、巨大残余位移 10.7% 等局域参数，直接证明 S 3p 上有显著自旋 / 电荷重排。这是区分 localized d⁸ 与 p-d hybridized d⁸ + d⁹L̲ 的关键。

    建立 ³³S 与 ³¹P 的互补判据

    ³¹P 主要反映 Ni 3d 磁矩，³³S 反映 S 3p 配体空穴。二者 Knight shift 温度依赖一致，证明 S 与 Ni 属于统一自旋系统；二者 T₁⁻¹ 行为相反，证明低能临界涨落不是普通自旋涨落，而是硫位点敏感的电荷 / EFG 涨落。这种“双核对照”显著提高了结论排他性。

    提出“向列电荷涨落驱动磁转变”的微观路径

    ³³S 归一化弛豫率满足 ³³R₁ ∝ |T − T₀|⁻⁰·⁴⁶⁴，且 T₀ = 152 K 接近 Tₙ = 155 K。该幂律发散被解释为由自旋双线性 Si·Sj 控制的配体电荷涨落，即临界向列涨落。这把 NiPS₃ 中的一级 AFM 转变、磁矩异常倾斜、单层 vestigial nematicity、磁激子相干性统一到同一自旋-电荷耦合框架中。

    对近期 Hund’s exciton 与局域 d⁸ 模型构成强约束

    2023–2025 年的多个模型仍以局域 d⁸ 或 d-d 激发为核心。该研究显示：任何忽略显著 d⁹L̲ ligand-hole admixture 的模型都难以解释 ³³S Ahf、νQ 和轨道 Knight shift。即便 Hund’s exciton 图像也需约 40% d⁹L̲ 成分，说明配体空穴不是可忽略修正，而是 NiPS₃ 低能物理的核心变量。

    领域地位

    该研究把 NiPS₃ 从“具有异常磁激子的范德华反铁磁体”推进为“具有可实验识别 Zhang-Rice triplet 基态和临界向列电荷涨落的自旋-电荷纠缠材料”。其主要价值不在发现新峰，而在提供决定性局域约束，使未来理论必须同时满足 p-d 强杂化、S 配体空穴、ZRT 自旋三重态、EFG 临界涨落、准二维向列性五个条件。

    阅读原文 ↗
    原文链接页内定位
  7. 07
    FePS3 中磁与晶格集体激发耦合#
    Coupling of magnetic and lattice collective excitations in the 2D van der Waals antiferromagnet FePS₃#
    📊 含图深析
    🧭 物理 / 凝聚态📖 arXiv / cond-mat👤 Kartik Panda, Itzik Kapon, Dumitru Dumcenco, Dirk van der Marel, Alexey Kuzmenko, Nimrod Bachar🔥 AI 82

    💡 亮点：FePS3 在 118 K 以下出现强磁-声子耦合谱特征。

    📖 展开分析 + 配图
    研究问题二维范德华反铁磁体 FePS₃ 中，zigzag 反铁磁序如何重塑低能集体激发：15 meV 磁激发是否与红外声子耦合、左右圆偏振光如何“看见”这种耦合、晶格振动是否能获得磁场依赖的磁光活性。
    创新方法将极化分辨红外磁透射、法拉第旋转和光学电导重构联合起来：用两条主光学极化轴分离各向异性声子，用 ±7 T 磁场追踪 122 cm⁻¹ 模的线性劈裂，再由绝对透射 + Faraday 角重构圆偏振光学电导，直接显示场劈裂磁激发的圆二色性；Aha 点是把“磁振子—声子耦合”从普通谱峰识别推进到圆偏振磁光响应和声子 Faraday 旋转层面。
    工作流程输入为 FePS₃ 薄片在 4–300 K、−7 至 +7 T、两条正交极化下的红外透射谱与 Faraday 旋转谱；先扫描极化角确定 Pol. 1/Pol. 2 主轴，再用 Drude–Lorentz 与 VDF 提取光学电导，结合 Raman 谱和 DFT 声子计算归属 Aᵤ/Bᵤ 声子；随后跟踪 122 cm⁻¹ 模的温度硬化、磁场劈裂和圆偏振电导，最终输出磁激发、声子各向异性、129 cm⁻¹ 杂化和声子磁光活性的耦合图谱。
    关键结果122.7 cm⁻¹ 激发在两种极化中频率和光谱权重几乎相同，随降温按 Néel 磁序参量硬化，并在磁场下以约 0.94 cm⁻¹/T 线性劈裂，确认其磁性起源；Tₙ 以下声子谱强烈各向异性，Pol. 1 中 146.7 cm⁻¹ 声子增强，Pol. 2 中对应权重降低约一个数量级并出现 160.3 cm⁻¹ 模；122 cm⁻¹ 附近 Faraday 旋转达 0.1–0.15 rad，远高于 2 mrad 灵敏度；129 cm⁻¹ 附近上支二色性减弱，指向磁振子与邻近红外声子杂化；多个声子也产生 Faraday 旋转，说明晶格振动获得磁场依赖光学活性。
    应用价值为二维反铁磁体中的自旋—晶格耦合提供可视化、可定量的光学探针，可用于识别磁激发、追踪磁相变、评估磁振子—声子混合强度，并为利用光、磁场和极化选择性调控二维磁体中的集体模、磁光器件和自旋电子学材料提供实验基础。

    第一部分：核心概览（Overview）

    FePS₃ 中磁激发—晶格振动耦合得到极化分辨红外磁透射、法拉第旋转和光学电导的联合刻画。122 cm⁻¹（15 meV）激发呈极化无关、随降温硬化、随磁场线性劈裂，确认为磁性集体模；邻近 129 cm⁻¹ 红外声子导致上支二色性减弱，显示磁振子—声子杂化。多个声子出现显著法拉第旋转，证明晶格振动获得磁场依赖光学活性。该工作把二维范德华反铁磁体中的各向异性自旋—声子耦合从谱线识别推进到圆偏振光学电导与磁光响应层面。

    ---

    第二部分：结构化快速回顾

    《Coupling of magnetic and lattice collective excitations in the 2D van der Waals antiferromagnet FePS₃》（None，）

    背景

    二维磁体为研究 Ising、XY、Kitaev、Heisenberg 等自旋模型提供平台。FePS₃ 是具有 zigzag antiferromagnetic order 的范德华反铁磁体，Néel 温度约 118–120 K，单层极限仍保持磁有序。已有中子散射发现 15 meV 与 40 meV 低能磁激发，但其与红外声子、圆偏振光学电导和晶格对称响应之间的关系仍不清楚。

    方法

    使用 polarization-resolved infrared magneto-transmission 与 Faraday rotation 测量 FePS₃ 的低能集体激发；样品为 26 μm 厚 FePS₃ 薄片。磁场范围 −7 T 到 +7 T，温度范围 4–300 K。透射谱用 Drude–Lorentz model 与 Variable Dielectric Function（VDF） 提取光学电导。辅助使用 Raman microscopy 和 DFT phonon calculations 进行模式归属。

    结果

    低于 Tₙ = 118 K 后，红外声子谱强烈各向异性：Pol. 1 中 146.7 cm⁻¹ 模增强，Pol. 2 中相近模式光谱权重降低约一个数量级；Pol. 2 出现 160.3 cm⁻¹ 模。122.7 cm⁻¹ 激发在两种极化中频率和权重相同，随降温按磁序参量形式硬化，并在磁场下以约 0.94 cm⁻¹/T 线性劈裂。法拉第旋转在 122 cm⁻¹ 附近达到 0.1–0.15 rad，远高于约 2 mrad 灵敏度。

    讨论

    Pol. 2 主要对应 Bᵤ modes / a-axis，Pol. 1 主要对应 Aᵤ modes / b-axis。122 cm⁻¹ 模的极化无关性区别于各向异性声子，支持其磁性起源。129 cm⁻¹ 附近声子与上支磁激发发生杂化，削弱圆二色响应。多个声子出现法拉第旋转，显示晶格振动被磁序赋予磁光活性。

    局限

    光学模型中假设 μ ≈ 1，未显式纳入磁导率贡献；Pol. 1/Pol. 2 未通过 XRD 与晶轴直接配准，而是由光学透射谱定义；部分低频精细结构无法被 Drude–Lorentz 拟合完整捕捉；122 cm⁻¹ 同时出现在 Raman 与 IR 中的选择定则问题仍未解决；40 meV 激发磁光强度弱，其微观机制仍待研究。

    结论

    FePS₃ 中低温反铁磁态伴随显著的声子各向异性、磁激发劈裂、圆偏振二色性和声子磁光活性。极化分辨磁光谱能够定量追踪二维反铁磁体中耦合的自旋—晶格动力学。

    ---

    第三部分：逐章节冷凝解析（Section-by-Section Condensing）

    Abstract

    Polarized magneto-optics maps coupled excitations

    通过极化红外磁透射和法拉第角旋转，FePS₃ 的集体激发在温度、磁场、极化维度上被系统映射。核心对象是二维范德华反铁磁体 FePS₃，Néel 温度约 118 K。摘要直接给出方法组合：*"We combine polarized infrared magneto-transmission and Faraday angle rotation measurements to map the collective excitations of the van der Waals antiferromagnet FePS₃."*

    Phonon anisotropy emerges below the Néel temperature

    低于 Tₙ ≈ 118 K 后，声子谱变得强烈各向异性，并与底层 zigzag antiferromagnetic order 对应。该各向异性不是高温晶格本征各向异性的简单延续，而是磁有序态中增强的光谱特征：*"Below the Néel temperature (Tₙ ≈ 118 K), the phonon spectrum becomes strongly anisotropic, reflecting the underlying zigzag antiferromagnetic order."*

    The 122 cm⁻¹ mode is magnetic rather than phononic

    122 cm⁻¹（15 meV） 激发具有三重判据：极化无关、降温硬化、磁场线性劈裂，因此被识别为磁性起源。摘要表述为：*"a prominent excitation at 122 cm⁻¹ (15 meV) is polarization-independent, hardens on cooling, and splits linearly with magnetic field, identifying its magnetic origin."*

    Circular optical conductivities reveal dichroism

    通过绝对透射和法拉第旋转，圆偏振光学电导被重构，场劈裂激发呈现显著二色性（dichroism）。核心实验创新不止是观察劈裂，而是从磁光数据得到圆偏振响应：*"From absolute transmission and Faraday rotation, we reconstruct the circular optical conductivities and reveal a pronounced dichroism of the field-split excitations."*

    The upper branch hybridizes with a nearby infrared phonon

    上支激发位于约 129 cm⁻¹，二色性响应减弱，解释为与附近红外声子发生杂化（hybridization）。摘要给出明确频率和物理图像：*"The upper branch near 129 cm⁻¹ exhibits a reduced dichroic response, consistent with hybridization with a nearby infrared phonon."*

    Phonons acquire magnetic-field-dependent optical activity

    多个声子模出现可观法拉第旋转，说明spin–phonon coupling 使晶格振动具有磁场依赖光学活性：*"Several phonon modes exhibit sizable Faraday rotation, providing evidence for spin-phonon coupling and demonstrating that lattice vibrations acquire magnetic-field-dependent optical activity."*

    Additional infrared excitations and a mid-infrared feature appear only in the magnetic state

    低于 Tₙ 后，红外谱出现额外激发；约 900 cm⁻¹ 的宽中红外特征只在磁有序态出现，指向磁态中晶格响应改变：*"additional excitations appear in the infrared spectra and a broad mid-infrared feature near 900 cm⁻¹ emerges only below Tₙ, consistent with a modified lattice response in the magnetic state."*

    Polarization-resolved magneto-optics becomes a probe of spin–lattice dynamics

    最终定位是方法学与材料物理双重贡献：FePS₃ 中的各向异性自旋—声子耦合被揭示，极化分辨磁光谱成为二维反铁磁体耦合动力学的强探针：*"These results highlight the anisotropic nature of spin–phonon coupling in FePS₃ and establish polarization-resolved magneto-optical spectroscopy as a powerful probe of coupled spin and lattice dynamics in two-dimensional antiferromagnets."*

    ---

    I Introduction

    2D magnets extend van der Waals physics beyond electronic properties

    二维材料研究从 graphene 和 transition-metal dichalcogenides 扩展到具有本征磁性的二维化合物，为自旋电子学和信息处理提供新材料基础。引言以领域背景开场：*"atomically thin crystals, from graphene to transition-metal dichalcogenides, have transformed condensed-matter research"*；二维磁体的重要性在于：*"an expanding family of two-dimensional (2D) compounds displays intrinsic magnetism, unlocking fresh opportunities for spintronic and information-processing technologies."*

    The unsolved issue is magnetic-order coupling to lattice dynamics

    尽管二维磁体制备、剥离、合成和器件集成已有进展，核心基础问题仍是磁有序如何耦合晶格动力学，以及这种耦合能否通过光学特征探测或控制。关键问题被明确表述为：*"fundamental questions remain about how magnetic order couples to lattice dynamics in 2D antiferromagnets, and whether unique optical signatures of spin–lattice interactions can be harnessed to probe or control magnetic phases."*

    2D magnets provide access to multiple spin-model universality classes

    二维磁体可以在单层尺度检验 Ising、XY、Kitaev、Heisenberg-type physics。这种平台允许外场调控基态：*"They permit direct access to Ising, XY, Kitaev, and Heisenberg-type physics within a single atomic layer"*，并可研究温度、磁场、应变和压力影响：*"external stimuli such as temperature, magnetic field, strain, and pressure modify the ground state."*

    FePS₃ is an Ising zigzag antiferromagnet among MPX₃ compounds

    MPX₃（M = Fe, Co, Ni, Mn; X = S, Se）是范德华磁体家族，包含不同自旋维度模型。FePS₃ 的 Tₙ 约 120 K，MnPS₃ 约 78 K，NiPS₃ 约 155 K，均具有 monoclinic C2/m 结构。FePS₃ 的模型和磁结构被清晰界定：*"FePS₃ adheres to an Ising model with a zigzag antiferromagnetic configuration, featuring in-plane ferromagnetic chains that are antiparallel along one of the in-plane crystal axes."* 对比而言：*"NiPS₃ and MnPS₃ are best described by an XY and Heisenberg model, respectively."*

    FePS₃ remains magnetic at the monolayer limit and is pressure tunable

    FePS₃ 的独特性包括单层仍保持磁有序，并可在准静水压力下发生绝缘体—金属转变：*"FePS₃ maintains its magnetic order at the monolayer limit"*；*"undergoes an insulator-to-metal transition under quasi-hydrostatic pressure."* 这些特征使其成为二维极限磁性和耦合自由度研究的模型体系。

    Known neutron excitations motivate optical study

    非弹性中子散射已识别 q = 0 处两个有能隙激发：15 meV 与 40 meV。引言直接给出：*"Inelastic neutron scattering measurements of FePS₃ have identified two excitations with finite gaps of 15 meV and 40 meV at q = 0."* 同时，FePS₃ 中自旋轨道耦合和晶场能量量级相当，有利于低能磁激发：*"the comparable magnitudes of spin-orbit coupling and crystal field energies in FePS₃ favor the presence of low-energy magnetic excitations."*

    The missing knowledge concerns phonon interaction, circular spectral weight, and symmetry effects

    现有知识缺口集中在三个方面：低能磁激发如何与声子相互作用、圆偏振光学电导光谱权重是多少、这些激发如何影响晶体对称性。问题被明确列为：*"a comprehensive understanding of how these low-energy magnetic excitations interact with phonons, what their circular-conductivity spectral weight is, and how they affect crystal symmetries in FePS₃ remains lacking."*

    Infrared spectroscopy gives direct access to collective-mode spectral weight

    红外光谱不仅适用于单层极限，也能直接测量磁相中不同集体模的光谱权重，从而评估耦合和物理起源。方法优势表述为：*"The advantage of optical spectroscopy is that it is also susceptible to the monolayer limit."* 红外的额外优势是：*"direct access to the spectral weight of the different collective modes in the magnetic phase and, as a result, to their coupling and their relation to the underlying physics of the magnetic state."*

    The study combines polarized spectroscopy and magneto-optical analysis

    研究目标是揭示 FePS₃ 反铁磁态中晶格振动与磁激发的相互作用，并确定 zigzag 自旋结构如何影响光学响应。方法目标概括为：*"we investigate the low-energy collective excitations of FePS₃ using polarization-resolved infrared magneto-transmission and Faraday rotation measurements."* 具体输出包括 122 cm⁻¹ 和 320 cm⁻¹ 磁激发的 Faraday rotation，以及圆偏振光学响应：*"report Faraday rotation measurements of the magnetic excitations at 122 cm⁻¹ and 320 cm⁻¹, enabling a quantitative determination of their circular optical response."*

    ---

    II Methods

    II.1 Sample preparation

    FePS₃ crystals were grown by chemical vapor transport

    FePS₃ 晶体使用 Chemical Vapor Transport（CVT） 生长，类似 MPX₃ 家族其他磁性范德华材料。方法原文为：*"FePS₃ crystals were grown by the Chemical Vapor Transport (CVT) method, like other magnetic van der Waals materials in the MPX3 group."*

    Stoichiometric Fe:P:S ratio and iodine transport agent were precisely specified

    原料比例为 Fe:P:S = 1:1:3，总质量约 0.5 g。纯度分别为 Fe 99.9%、P 99.99%、S 99.999%。碘作为传输剂，浓度约 2 mg/cm³。实验细节为：*"A stoichiometric amount in the ratio 1:1:3 of elements Fe (99.9%, Chempure), P (99.99%, Alfa Aesar), and S (99.999%, Fluka), corresponding to approximately 0.5 gram total mass, was inserted in a quartz tube inside a glove box, together with approximately 2 mg/cm³ of iodine as transport agent."*

    Growth used evacuated sealed quartz tubes and a 680/630 °C gradient

    石英管抽真空至 10⁻⁴ mbar，中间进行 Ar 冲洗，封管长度 16 cm。炉温梯度为热端 680 °C、冷端 630 °C，生长时间 20 days。原文给出：*"The tube was subsequently evacuated down to 10⁻⁴ mbar, with intermediate Ar flushing, and sealed to a length of 16 cm."* 以及：*"in a controlled temperature gradient with 680 °C and 630 °C for the hot and cold ends, respectively."* 生长周期为：*"At the end of 20 days, the furnace was switched off, and the crystals were extracted from the tube."*

    ---

    II.2 Infrared spectroscopy

    FTIR magneto-optical setup covered temperature, field, and polarization dependence

    红外磁光系综使用 Bruker Vertex 70v FTIR 与 Cryogenic magneto-optical cryostat，可测温度、磁场、入射/出射极化依赖透射。原文为：*"we have used a Bruker Vertex 70v Fourier Transform Infra-Red (FTIR) spectrometer coupled to a Cryogenic magneto-optical cryostat, allowing transmission measurements as a function of temperature, magnetic field, and incoming/outgoing polarization."*

    FIR and MIR sources were Hg arc lamp and Globar

    远红外使用 Hg arc lamp，中红外使用 Globar（SiC）。由于残余磁场影响汞弧灯，低于 40 cm⁻¹ 的测量可靠性受限，因此主要呈现 Globar 数据。原文为：*"We have used Hg arc lamp and Globar (SiC) sources for the far-infrared (FIR) and mid-infrared (MIR) frequency ranges, respectively."* 以及：*"Residual magnetic fields affect the arc lamp, limiting reliable measurements below 40 cm⁻¹."*

    Detector coverage spanned 10–4000 cm⁻¹

    透射强度检测使用多个液氦冷却 Si bolometer：10–80 cm⁻¹、40–700 cm⁻¹、500–4000 cm⁻¹。原始细节为：*"an IR Labs liquid-helium-cooled (and pumped) Si bolometer with cutoff filter for the range of 10 to 80 cm⁻¹"*；*"an IR Labs liquid-helium-cooled Si bolometer with a cutoff filter for the range of 40 to 700 cm⁻¹"*；*"three different cutoff filters covering the range of 500 to 4000 cm⁻¹."*

    Faraday geometry used ±7 T magnetic fields

    磁场可调范围为 −7 T 到 +7 T，并在 Faraday 构型中平行于光传播方向、垂直于样品表面法线。表述为：*"The magnetic field of the cryostat can be tuned from -7 T to +7 T and was aligned parallel (perpendicular) to the light propagation vector (sample surface normal) in the Faraday configuration."*

    Temperature range and reference acquisition were controlled in situ

    样品座温度范围 4 K 到约 300 K。样品用银胶固定，并位于超导磁体真空腔内。线性平移台允许在同一温度、磁场、极化条件下测样品和空孔/镜面参考：*"The temperature range of the cryostat sample holder is from 4 K to about 300 K"*；*"allowing the measurement of a sample in transmission (reflection) configuration and a bare hole (mirror) reference at any desired temperature, magnetic field, and incoming/outgoing polarization."*

    Polarization-dependent transmission required principal optical axes

    非偏振透射拟合失败，说明 FePS₃ 磁态中单斜晶体各向异性不可忽略。原文为：*"Our preliminary attempts to measure and fit non-polarized transmission data and, as a result, to extract the optical conductivity have failed, indicating the importance of the polarization dependence of the transmission spectrum and the anisotropy of the monoclinic crystal of FePS₃ in the magnetic state."*

    Two principal optical polarizations were defined spectroscopically rather than crystallographically

    在 5 K、0 T 下扫描极化角后，识别出相差 90° 的两个主透射谱，称为 Pol 1 与 Pol 2。它们未通过 XRD 与 a–b 晶轴绑定，而由光谱定义：*"We have identified two distinct transmission spectra separated by a 90° polarizer angle difference, to which we refer here as 'Pol 1' and 'Pol 2'."* 限定条件为：*"these two principal polarizations were not associated with the a-b plane crystal axis using the X-ray diffraction apparatus and are only determined by the optical transmission spectra."*

    Fast Faraday protocol was vulnerable to birefringence artifacts

    常规快速 Faraday 协议只测 ±B 和 A = P = ±45° 四种组合，但 FePS₃ 单斜结构和反铁磁态光学各向异性会引入双折射伪影。原文指出：*"the typical fast protocol procedure ... was subject to possible birefringence artifacts."*

    Full Faraday protocol scanned a 360° polarizer rotation

    为避免伪影，完整协议固定 analyzer 在一个主角度，同时入射 polarizer 以 15° 间隔旋转完整 360°；测量在 5 K 和 B = ±7 T 下进行。原文为：*"the analyzer angle is fixed to one of the principal angles while measurement of the transmission intensity is being taken at intervals of 15° for a full 360° polarizer rotation."* 以及：*"conducted the full protocol at a temperature of 5 K ... and at fields of B = ±7 T."*

    ---

    II.3 Raman microscopy

    Raman spectroscopy used 532 nm excitation and cryogenic temperature control

    Raman 测量使用 LabRAM HR Evolution Horiba Confocal Raman Microscope 与 CryoVac liquid helium flow cryostat。激发光为 532 nm 非偏振激光，经 63× Olympus objective 聚焦，功率 0.4 mW。原文为：*"A 532-nm unpolarized laser was used as the excitation source, focused on the sample ... through a 63× Olympus objective, and the laser power was set to 0.4 mW throughout the experiment."*

    Detection used Czerny–Turner spectrometer and LN₂-cooled CCD

    散射光由同一物镜收集，经 analyzer 后进入 Czerny-Turner spectrometer，光栅为 600 或 1800 grooves/mm，探测器为液氮冷却 CCD。原文为：*"sent to a Czerny-Turner spectrometer equipped with either a 600- or 1800-grooves-per-mm grating, and was detected by a liquid nitrogen-cooled CCD array."*

    Temperature-dependent Raman spectra covered 300 K to 5 K

    温度从 300 K 到 10 K，间隔 10 K，另加 5 K 基温测量。原文为：*"The spectra were obtained as a function of temperature from 300 K down to 10 K at 10 K intervals, in addition to a measurement at 5 K."*

    High-resolution grating targeted the 80–130 cm⁻¹ low-energy region

    1800 grooves/mm 光栅测量弹性线附近约 ±600 cm⁻¹ 的 Stokes/anti-Stokes 区域，尤其用于解析 80–130 cm⁻¹、相变以下出现的模式。原文为：*"The 1800 grooves per mm grating was used to measure the Raman shift spectrum in the range of about ±600 cm⁻¹ ... in particular the modes around 80 to 130 cm⁻¹ appearing below the phase transition of FePS₃."*

    Wide-range grating targeted excitations near 1000 cm⁻¹

    600 grooves/mm 光栅覆盖至约 4000 cm⁻¹，用于观察此前报道中约 1000 cm⁻¹ 的激发。原文为：*"The 600 grooves per mm grating was used to measure the large Raman shift range of up to approximately 4000 cm⁻¹ in order to resolve the excitations ... around 1000 cm⁻¹."*

    ---

    II.4 Phonon calculation

    DFT phonon calculations used Quantum ESPRESSO PWscf v6.6

    声子频率由第一性原理 DFT 计算获得，软件为 Quantum ESPRESSO PWscf v6.6。原文为：*"we have performed first-principles Density-functional theory (DFT) calculations with the Quantum ESPRESSO PWscf ... package v6.6."*

    Exchange–correlation and pseudopotentials were specified

    交换关联使用 PBE functional 与 GGA。赝势为 Fe 的 PAW，P 和 S 的 Ultrasoft，均与 PBE 一致：*"Exchange–correlation effects were treated within the PBE ... functional and the generalized-gradient approximation (GGA)."* 以及：*"Scalar-relativistic pseudopotentials ... PAW ... for Fe and US ... for P and S."*

    Numerical parameters controlled convergence

    晶格参数来自 Materials Project。波函数和电荷密度能量截断分别为 90 Ry 与 1080 Ry。占据使用 Marzari–Vanderbilt cold smearing，宽度 0.0147 Ry（≈0.20 eV）。k 网格为 6×4×3 Monkhorst–Pack。自洽混合参数 β = 0.4，收敛阈值 8×10⁻⁹ Ry，20 次 SCF 达收敛。原文细节包括：*"Wavefunctions and charge density were expanded with kinetic-energy cutoffs of 90 Ry and 1080 Ry, respectively."*；*"Brillouin-zone sampling employed a Monkhorst–Pack 6×4×3 mesh."*；*"convergence was reached in 20 SCF iterations."*

    Paramagnetic FePS₃ phonons decompose into Raman and infrared irreducible representations

    FePS₃ 属单斜 C2/m 空间群，点群 C₂h。Γ 点光学声子分解为 Γ = 8Aᵍ + 7Bᵍ + 6Aᵤ + 9Bᵤ；Aᵍ/Bᵍ Raman 活性，Aᵤ/Bᵤ IR 活性。原文为：*"FePS₃ crystallizes in the monoclinic space group C2/m (point group C₂h) of the paramagnetic state"*；*"the optical phonons at the Γ point decompose as Γ = 8A_g + 7B_g + 6Aᵤ + 9Bᵤ."*

    Zigzag antiferromagnetism was modeled by collinear spin polarization

    磁结构包含沿 a-axis 的铁磁 zigzag 链、沿 b-axis 和 c-axis 的反铁磁耦合。计算用 nₛₚᵢₙ = 2，两个 Fe 子晶格初始反平行，Fe1/Fe2 初始磁化 ±0.3125，P/S 给 0.1 小种子磁化。原文为：*"we have tried to capture this structure with a collinear spin polarization (nₛₚᵢₙ₌₂₎ of two Fe sublattices in the a-b plane initialized antiparallel (Fe1/Fe2 starting magnetization ±0.3125), and small seed magnetizations on P and S (0.1)."*

    The converged magnetic cell had zero net moment and large absolute magnetization

    计算单胞含 20 atoms、四种元素。自洽后总磁矩约 0 μB/cell，绝对磁化约 15 μB，符合反铁磁补偿。原文为：*"calculations were performed for 20 atoms per cell across four atomic species."* 以及：*"The converged self-consistent solution has essentially zero net moment with total magnetization ≈0 μB per cell (absolute magnetization ∼15 μB)."*

    Magnetic-cell phonons doubled the number of modes

    使用 QE 的 ph.x 计算 Γ 点声子；由于磁性单胞较常规顺磁单胞更大，得到的模式数加倍。原文为：*"Phonons were computed within density-functional theory (DFT) as implemented in QE’s ph.x and resulted in zone-center (Γ-point) phonon frequencies with twice the number of modes compared to the conventional paramagnetic cell calculation."*

    Mode assignments combine polarization-resolved infrared data and DFT

    表 1 中红外声子对称性基于极化分辨红外实验并与 DFT 比较；Raman 结果及 DFT 归属在附录表 2。原文为：*"The symmetry assignments used in Table 1 are based on polarization-resolved infrared measurements and compared with DFT calculations."*

    ---

    III Results

    III.1 Optical Conductivity

    Polarized optical conductivity of FePS₃ is reported for the first time

    FePS₃ 的偏振透射和偏振光学电导结果为首次报告，用于分离磁态中集体激发、声子与晶体对称性的关系。原文明确写道：*"The polarized transmission and the polarized optical conductivity results in this work are reported here for the first time for FePS₃."*

    Above Tₙ, two principal polarizations are nearly identical

    在显著高于 Tₙ = 118 K 的温度下，两条主极化轴的透射谱没有主要差异。原文为：*"the transmission spectra at temperatures substantially higher than the Néel antiferromagnetic transition temperature, T_N = 118 K, of FePS₃ show no major difference between the two principal polarization measurement axes."*

    Below Tₙ, new low-frequency absorptions and a 900 cm⁻¹ feature emerge

    低于 Tₙ 后，在 <200 cm⁻¹ 区域出现多条新吸收线，其中 122 cm⁻¹（15 meV） 模在两种极化均出现；约 900 cm⁻¹ 宽吸收仅在 Pol. 1 出现。原文为：*"Below T_N, the transmission spectra exhibit several new absorption lines in the low frequency range (<200 cm⁻¹), among them is a mode at 122 cm⁻¹ (15 meV), in both polarizations, and a wide absorption feature at around 900 cm⁻¹ appearing only in the 1st polarization."*

    Transmission data were modeled by a plane-parallel Drude–Lorentz slab

    40–4000 cm⁻¹ 范围的透射谱使用平行平板模型与 Drude–Lorentz dielectric function 拟合：

    [

    ǎrepsilon(ømega)=ǎrepsilonᵢₙfty+sumⱼ fracømegaₚ_ⱼ²ømega₀_ⱼ²⁻ømega²⁻ⁱγⱼømega

    ]

    可提取每个模式的 central frequency ω₀、plasma frequency ωp 和 width γ。原文为：*"from which we obtain the central frequency ω₀, plasma frequency ωp, and width γ of each mode j."*

    The optical analysis assumed μ ≈ 1

    模型假设磁导率 μ ≈ 1，这是磁性半导体红外研究中的常见近似，但更完整的含磁导率处理留待未来。原文为：*"We note that this analysis assumes μ ≈ 1."* 以及：*"A more complete treatment, including magnetic permeability effects, is left for future work."*

    At 150 K, four strong infrared modes appear for each polarization

    在 150 K > Tₙ，Pol. 1 的强模位于 144、186.1、256.1、571.8 cm⁻¹；Pol. 2 位于 149.5、185、260.1、573.4 cm⁻¹。原文给出：*"At 150 K we detect four strong modes for each polarization situated at 144, 186.1, 256.1, and 571.8 cm⁻¹ for the 1st polarization and 149.5, 185, 260.1, and 573.4 cm⁻¹ for the 2nd polarization."*

    Low-temperature strong modes connect to high-temperature phonons

    在 5 K 反铁磁态，Pol. 1 中 184.7、257.6、573.4 cm⁻¹ 和 Pol. 2 中 189.4、260.4、574.9 cm⁻¹ 与高温模式频率接近，因此归属为对应声子延续。原文为：*"The strong modes at 184.7, 257.6, and 573.4 cm⁻¹ for the 1st polarization and 189.4, 260.4, and 574.9 cm⁻¹ for the 2nd polarization are associated with the modes above T_N."*

    A major anisotropy appears near 147–150 cm⁻¹

    反铁磁态中 147.3 cm⁻¹ 模在 Pol. 1 是强 IR 峰，而 Pol. 2 中 149.5 cm⁻¹ 模相较 Tₙ 以上振子强度降低约一个数量级。原文为：*"the 147.3 cm⁻¹ mode is observed as a strong IR peak in the 1st polarization, while the 149.5 cm⁻¹ mode in the 2nd polarization shows a substantial decrease in the optical conductivity by about one order of magnitude compared to its oscillator strength above T_N."*

    The 215 cm⁻¹ infrared mode is primarily Pol. 2 active and enhanced in the AFM state

    215 cm⁻¹ 模在相变以上已存在，主要在 Pol. 2 活跃，并在反铁磁态增强。原文为：*"the mode at 215 cm⁻¹, observed above the phase transition, is mainly active in the 2nd polarization and is further enhanced in the antiferromagnetic state."*

    Drude–Lorentz fitting cannot capture all fine low-frequency structures

    低频范围内、尤其相变以下新特征附近，Drude–Lorentz 模型无法完整捕捉细节；典型困难包括 Pol. 1 的 128 和 133 cm⁻¹ 吸收线、Pol. 2 的约 158 cm⁻¹ 特征。原文为：*"The Drude-Lorenz fit is, however, not capturing all the fine details of the transmission spectra"*；*"particularly evident in the absorption lines at 128 and 133 cm⁻¹ in the 1st polarization, and at about 158 cm⁻¹ in the 2nd polarization."*

    VDF was used to obtain fuller temperature- and polarization-dependent conductivity

    为克服 Drude–Lorentz 局限，使用 Variable Dielectric Function（VDF） 处理原始透射数据，覆盖两种主极化和 150 K 到 5 K 全部温度。原文为：*"we have employed the Variable Dielectric Function (VDF) method to the raw transmission data for both principal polarizations and at all measured temperatures from 150 K down to 5 K."*

    VDF conductivity confirms low-energy phonon anisotropy

    VDF 提取的实部光学电导 σ₁ 显示反铁磁相变以下强烈各向异性，尤其低能区。Pol. 1 中 146.7 cm⁻¹ 强声子在 Pol. 2 光谱权重显著降低；Pol. 1 中 128 cm⁻¹ IR 模突出，Pol. 2 中 160 cm⁻¹ 模独有。原文为：*"the strong phonon mode at 146.7 cm⁻¹ in Pol. 1 exhibits a significantly reduced spectral weight in Pol. 2."* 以及：*"the IR mode at 128 cm⁻¹ is prominent in Pol. 1, while a distinct mode at 160 cm⁻¹ appears only in Pol. 2."*

    Mode assignments are indicative rather than rigorous

    表 1 的对称性归属基于实验频率与 DFT 频率最接近匹配，不应视为严格群论分类。原文为：*"the symmetry assignments are indicative, based on the closest correspondence between experimental frequencies and DFT calculations, and should not be interpreted as a rigorous symmetry classification."*

    Table 1 identifies many low-temperature infrared excitations

    5 K 下观测到大量 IR 激发，重要条目包括：

    • 52 cm⁻¹：Pol. 1/2，宽 IR 特征。原注释：*"Wide IR feature; Ref. [33]."*
    • 102.3 cm⁻¹：Pol. 2，对应 DFT 101.9 Bᵤ。
    • 108.1 cm⁻¹：Pol. 1，宽 IR 特征且显示 Faraday angle。原注释：*"Wide IR feature; Shows Faraday angle."*
    • 119.5 cm⁻¹：Pol. 1，为 122.7 cm⁻¹ 的肩峰。原注释：*"IR shoulder of 122.7 cm⁻¹ in Pol. 1."*
    • 122.7 cm⁻¹：Pol. 1/2，磁激发。原注释：*"Magnetic excitation."*
    • 128.5 cm⁻¹：Pol. 1，对应 DFT 129.7 Aᵤ。
    • 133.1 cm⁻¹：Pol. 1/2，显示 Faraday angle。
    • 146.7 cm⁻¹：Pol. 1，强 IR 模，对应 δsPX₃。原注释：*"Strong IR mode in Pol. 1; δsPX₃ mode."*
    • 160.3 cm⁻¹：Pol. 2，对应 DFT 161.7 Bᵤ。
    • 165.6 cm⁻¹：Pol. 2，对应 DFT 167.6 Bᵤ，显示 Faraday angle。
    • 184.7 cm⁻¹：Pol. 1，强 IR 模，对应 R′xyPX₃。
    • 189.3 cm⁻¹：Pol. 2，强 IR 模。
    • 215.4 cm⁻¹：Pol. 1/2，对应 DFT 211.8 Aᵤ。
    • 257.6 cm⁻¹：Pol. 1，对应 DFT 254.6 Aᵤ，强 IR 模，对应 δdPX₃。
    • 260.1 cm⁻¹：Pol. 2，强 IR 模。
    • 532–575 cm⁻¹ 区域：多条高频 IR 模，其中 573.5 cm⁻¹ Pol. 1 和 575 cm⁻¹ Pol. 2 为强 IR 模。

    ---

    III.2 The 122 cm⁻¹ Excitation in FePS₃

    The 122 cm⁻¹ excitation is isotropic despite phonon anisotropy

    虽然声子谱强烈各向异性，122 cm⁻¹ 模在两种极化中以相同频率和相同光谱权重出现，实验分辨率约 0.5 cm⁻¹。这与晶格振动模的各向异性形成对照。原文为：*"the mode at 122 cm⁻¹ ... is present in both polarizations with the same spectral weight and at the same frequency, up to the spectral resolution of our measurements (about 0.5 cm⁻¹)."* 结论为：*"This is consistent with the 122 cm⁻¹ excitation being isotropic in FePS₃ compared to the aforementioned lattice vibrational modes."*

    Prior literature identifies the 122 cm⁻¹ excitation as a magnon

    该激发此前已被识别为 FePS₃ 的 122 cm⁻¹ magnon，且与 Fe 3d⁶ multiplet structure 有关。原文为：*"identified previously as the 122 cm⁻¹ magnon of FePS₃"*；*"is inherent to the Fe 3d⁶ multiplet structure."*

    The excitation appears in both Raman and infrared spectra

    5 K、0 T 下，该激发同时出现在 Raman shift 和红外透射谱中。原文为：*"the excitation at 122 cm⁻¹ appears in both the Raman shift and the infrared spectra."* 这在选择定则上可能暗示奇偶模混合，但 FePS₃ 反铁磁态中反演对称性仍保持。

    Raman–IR coexistence does not necessarily mean inversion symmetry breaking

    尽管同一激发同时 IR 与 Raman 活性常被理解为反演对称破缺，但 FePS₃ AFM 态保持 inversion symmetry。原文谨慎表述：*"Although this excitation is observed in both IR and Raman spectroscopy, which might imply inversion symmetry breaking resulting in the mixing of odd and even modes, it is important to note that inversion symmetry is preserved in FePS₃ at the AFM state."* 解释仍开放：*"the interpretation of these observations remains an open question."*

    The 122 cm⁻¹ central frequency follows a magnetic order-parameter-like temperature dependence

    该模随降温硬化，且两种极化温度依赖相同。拟合使用：

    [

    ømega₀₍T)=a ḑot tanhłeft[1.82łeft(1.018łeft(fracT_NT-1i̊ght)i̊ght)⁰.⁵i̊ght]+c

    ]

    其中 Tₙ = 118 K。原文为：*"The mode hardens as the temperature is lowered and follows the same temperature dependence for both principal polarizations."* 以及：*"the temperature dependence resembles that of an order parameter change."*

    Fit parameters are nearly identical for Pol 1 and Pol 2

    拟合得到 Pol. 1：a = 33.39 ± 0.87, c = 89.13 ± 0.80；Pol. 2：a = 33.94 ± 1.01, c = 87.98 ± 0.94。图注给出：*"The fitting yields a = 33.39 ± 0.87, c = 89.13 ± 0.80 (Pol 1) and a = 33.94 ± 1.01, c = 87.98 ± 0.94 (Pol 2)."* 这支持极化无关的磁序参量行为。

    Order-parameter tracking establishes AFM-state origin

    122 cm⁻¹ 模的中心频率跟随具有 Tₙ 的磁序参量温度依赖，清楚说明该激发源于反铁磁态。原文为：*"The mode’s central frequency ω₀ follows the temperature dependence of a magnetic order parameter with transition temperature T_N and provides clear evidence that the 122 cm⁻¹ excitation originates at the antiferromagnetic state."*

    Magnetic-field splitting provides a second magnetic-origin criterion

    该模在磁场下劈裂成两支，与近期 Raman 和光谱研究一致。原文为：*"the excitation ... splits into two modes as a function of the magnetic field."* 以及：*"Figure 7 shows the field-induced splitting of the 122 cm⁻¹ mode in our transmission spectra."*

    The splitting is resolved up to 7 T and follows free-electron-like gyromagnetic behavior

    在最高 7 T 的磁场下劈裂清晰可分辨，斜率对应约 γ ≈ 0.94 cm⁻¹/T 的陀螺磁比。原文为：*"This splitting becomes clearly resolved at fields up to 7 T."* 图 8 说明：*"The dashed line represents the expected linear dependence assuming a gyromagnetic ratio (γ ≈ 0.94 cm⁻¹/T)."*

    Higher-field deviations arise from avoided crossings

    高场下线性关系会因集体模相互作用和 avoided crossing 失效，尤其低能支与 108 cm⁻¹ Raman mode 的相互作用。原文为：*"this field dependence breaks down at higher magnetic fields due to the avoided crossing of two modes, the lower energy mode’s branch and the Raman mode at 108 cm⁻¹."*

    ---

    III.3 Faraday Angle Rotation

    Faraday rotation at 5 K and ±7 T is newly reported for FePS₃

    FePS₃ 在 5 K、B = ±7 T 下的法拉第角旋转此前未被报道。原文为：*"we show in Figure 9 the Faraday angle rotation at 5 K and fields of B = ±7 T, which was not reported before for FePS₃, to the best of our knowledge."*

    The full protocol was used for both principal optical axes

    Faraday 角通过完整协议获得，覆盖两条主极化轴，目的是避免由各向异性和双折射造成的伪影。原文为：*"The measurement was obtained using the full protocol for the two principal axes used in this work."*

    Low-transmission regions were masked to avoid artifacts

    透射低于 1% 的光谱区被遮蔽，因为信号过低时 Faraday 角提取不可靠。该阈值高于仪器灵敏度下限。原文为：*"we masked out spectral regions where the transmission coefficient dropped below 1%."* 以及：*"This threshold lies above the sensitivity limit of our experimental setup, ensuring the reliability of the Faraday angle measurements."*

    The split 122 cm⁻¹ excitation produces large Faraday rotation

    劈裂后的 122 cm⁻¹ 磁激发在 5 K、7 T 下产生约 0.1–0.15 rad 的 Faraday rotation，远大于约 2 mrad 的测量灵敏度。原文为：*"The 122 cm⁻¹ excitation that splits into two modes shows a Faraday angle rotation of about 0.1 to 0.15 rad at 5 K and 7 T."* 以及：*"This Faraday angle is much larger than the sensitivity of the measurements setup (about 2 mRad)."*

    Several phonons also show Faraday rotation

    图 9 中不仅 122 cm⁻¹ 磁激发显示 Faraday 特征，多个声子也出现显著 Faraday rotation，证明磁有序态中晶格模与自旋相耦合。图注总结为：*"Pronounced Faraday rotation features appear at the 122 cm⁻¹ excitation ... as well as at several phonon modes, highlighting strong spin–phonon coupling in the antiferromagnetic state."*

    A weak Faraday feature near 320 cm⁻¹ corresponds to the 40 meV magnetic excitation

    FePS₃ 已知存在约 40 meV 高能磁激发。Faraday 谱在约 320 cm⁻¹ 处出现弱特征，被归属为该高能磁激发。原文为：*"FePS₃ has another magnetic excitation at higher energies of about 40 meV."* 以及：*"A close examination of our Faraday angle rotation spectrum near that energy reveals a very weak feature, which we attribute to this high-energy magnetic excitation."*

    The 320 cm⁻¹ feature strengthens and shifts on cooling below Tₙ

    在接近 Tₙ 下方时，该 Faraday 特征难以高于噪声；深入反铁磁相后，约 320 cm⁻¹ 出现 dip，随降温强度增加并发生频移。原文为：*"Below T_N but still close to the phase transition, it is very hard to detect any Faraday angle rotation above our measurement baseline and within the noise level; however, as the system goes deep into the antiferromagnetic phase, a dip in the data appears at about 320 cm⁻¹."* 结论为：*"The appearance of a Faraday rotation signal at 320 cm⁻¹, accompanied by a temperature-dependent shift and an intensity increase, provides evidence that this feature originates from a magnetic excitation."*

    Optical and neutron energies agree despite momentum-selection differences

    光学谱通常只对 q ≈ 0 集体激发敏感；中子散射中 122 cm⁻¹ / 15 meV 对应 commensurate q = (0,1,0)，色散到 q = (0,0.5,0) 约 17 meV。40 meV 激发出现在 incommensurate q = (±1,k,∓1/3)，并在 q = (±2,k,∓2/3) 等处色散到约 17 meV。原文强调：*"In general, optical spectroscopy is sensitive only to q ≈ 0 collective excitations."* 但能量一致：*"the frequencies at which we measure the Faraday angle rotation signal agree with the excitation energies of FePS₃ as measured by inelastic neutron scattering."*

    The intensity contrast between 15 meV and 40 meV excitations remains unresolved

    122 cm⁻¹（15 meV）与 320 cm⁻¹（40 meV）Faraday 强度差异已被实验观察，但微观来源未知。原文为：*"the difference in intensity between the excitations at 122 cm⁻¹ (15 meV) and 320 cm⁻¹ (40 meV) is observed experimentally; however, its microscopic origin remains an open question and requires further investigation."*

    ---

    IV Discussion

    IV.1 Crystal Symmetries in FePS₃

    FePS₃ retains monoclinic C2/m symmetry and inversion symmetry

    FePS₃ 在顺磁态具有单斜 C2/m 结构与 C₂h 点群，二重旋转轴沿 b-axis，镜面位于 ac plane。分析中不假设对称性降低，反演对称性保持。原文为：*"FePS₃ has a monoclinic C2/m structure and C₂h space group in the paramagnetic state, with a twofold rotation axis along b and a mirror plane in the ac plane."* 以及：*"The structure also preserves inversion symmetry, and no symmetry lowering is assumed in the present analysis."*

    High-temperature transmission is nearly isotropic despite intrinsic lattice anisotropy

    虽然晶格本征各向异性存在，但在 T = 150 K、即 Tₙ 以上，两种极化透射谱近似各向同性，只有若干声子频率差异可达数 cm⁻¹，尤其 145、185、255、570 cm⁻¹ 附近。原文为：*"Although the lattice is intrinsically anisotropic, the transmission spectra appear nearly isotropic above T_N (e.g., at T = 150 K) for both polarizations, with only small differences in phonon energies of up to several cm⁻¹."*

    Infrared-active modes are Aᵤ and Bᵤ with different dipole directions

    在 C₂h 对称性中，IR 活性声子属于 Aᵤ 与 Bᵤ 不可约表示，分别对应平行和垂直于 b-axis 的偶极矩。原文为：*"the infrared-active phonons belong to the Aᵤ and Bᵤ irreducible representations, corresponding to dipole moments parallel and perpendicular to the crystallographic b-axis, respectively."*

    Polarization-resolved infrared spectroscopy probes directional lattice dynamics

    由于 Aᵤ 和 Bᵤ 对应不同偶极方向，极化分辨红外谱可以直接读取晶格动力学方向性。原文为：*"Accordingly, polarization-resolved infrared spectroscopy directly probes the directional character of the lattice dynamics."*

    Aᵤ modes correspond to b-axis displacements and Bᵤ modes to ac-plane motion

    Aᵤ 模与沿 b-axis 的位移相关；Bᵤ 模涉及 ac plane 内运动，低能区预期有更多 P₂S₆ units 的变形与 librational modes。原文为：*"The Aᵤ modes are associated with displacements along the b-axis, while the Bᵤ modes involve motion within the ac plane."* 以及：*"a larger number of deformation and librational modes of the P₂S₆ units are expected at low energies."*

    Pol. 2 is mainly Bᵤ/a-axis and Pol. 1 mainly Aᵤ/b-axis

    实验极化谱与 DFT 比较显示 Pol. 2 主要对应 Bᵤ modes，因此关联 a-axis；Pol. 1 主要对应 Aᵤ modes，关联 b-axis。原文为：*"Comparing the polarized spectra with the DFT phonon calculations indicates that Pol. 2 is predominantly associated with Bᵤ modes and therefore with the a-axis, while Pol. 1 corresponds mainly to Aᵤ modes and the b-axis."*

    Richer Pol. 2 low-energy phonons support Bᵤ assignment

    Pol. 2 在 250 cm⁻¹ 以下显示更丰富低能声子结构，符合 Bᵤ vibrations 的面内性质。原文为：*"This assignment is supported by the richer low-energy phonon structure observed in Pol. 2 below 250 cm⁻¹, consistent with the in-plane character of the Bᵤ vibrations."*

    DFT frequencies partly revise earlier phonon assignments

    此前 Bernasconi 等预测 150、221、258、570 cm⁻¹ 附近存在 Aᵤ/Bᵤ doublets；当前计算得到对应频率有所不同。例如 570 cm⁻¹ 实验模对应计算 550 cm⁻¹（Bᵤ） 和 556 cm⁻¹（Aᵤ）；258 cm⁻¹ 和 150 cm⁻¹ 实验模对应计算约 254 cm⁻¹ 和 154 cm⁻¹。原文为：*"Bernasconi et al. predicted Aᵤ and Bᵤ doublets near 150, 221, 258, and 570 cm⁻¹."* 以及：*"the mode near 570 cm⁻¹ corresponds to calculated modes at 550 cm⁻¹ (Bᵤ₎ and 556 cm⁻¹ (Aᵤ₎."*

    Calculated 178/179 cm⁻¹ modes better match observed features than the older 221 cm⁻¹ assignment

    当前计算得到 178 cm⁻¹（Aᵤ） 和 179 cm⁻¹（Bᵤ），比此前建议的 221 cm⁻¹ 更接近实验观测特征。原文为：*"our calculations yield modes at 178 cm⁻¹ (Aᵤ₎ and 179 cm⁻¹ (Bᵤ₎, which are closer to the experimentally observed features than the previously suggested 221 cm⁻¹ mode."*

    ---

    第四部分：深度理解与语言支持（Understanding & Nuance）

    1. 术语解析

    Collective excitations

    Collective excitations 指多体系统中许多自由度协同振荡产生的准粒子或模式，不是单个电子、单个离子或单个自旋的孤立运动。在该研究中包括声子（phonons）、磁激发/磁振子（magnons）以及可能的混合模。语境中的 *"map the collective excitations"* 不只是“找到谱峰”，而是测量其频率、温度依赖、磁场劈裂、极化选择性和磁光响应。

    Polarization-independent

    Polarization-independent 在这里是判别 122 cm⁻¹ 激发性质的关键。普通红外声子会因晶体方向和偶极矩方向不同而在 Pol. 1/Pol. 2 中强弱差异显著；122 cm⁻¹ 在两种极化中频率和光谱权重相同，说明它不像普通晶格振动那样被红外偶极方向强烈约束，更符合磁性集体激发。

    Dichroism

    Dichroism（二色性） 指材料对两种圆偏振光（通常 σ⁺ 与 σ⁻）吸收或光学电导不同。这里的二色性来自磁场劈裂后的激发对左右圆偏振选择定则不同。*"pronounced dichroism of the field-split excitations"* 的重点是圆偏振光学响应不对称，而不是简单的线偏振各向异性。

    Hybridization

    Hybridization（杂化） 指两个能量相近、对称性允许耦合的模式不再保持纯粹身份，而形成混合本征态。129 cm⁻¹ 附近上支磁激发与红外声子相互作用，使其圆二色响应减弱；这意味着该支激发含有更多晶格成分，磁光选择性被“稀释”。

    Avoided crossing

    Avoided crossing（反交叉） 指两个模式随外参量变化本应能量相交，但因耦合而相互排斥，形成能隙并交换部分谱权重。文中提到高磁场下 122 cm⁻¹ 低能支与 108 cm⁻¹ Raman mode 发生 avoided crossing，因此简单线性 Zeeman 劈裂关系失效。

    ---

    2. 疑难查证

    为什么 122 cm⁻¹ 同时出现在 Raman 和 IR 中会引起选择定则问题？

    在具有反演对称性的晶体中，中心对称选择定则通常导致 Raman-active 与 IR-active 模互斥：偶宇称（gerade）模 Raman 活性，奇宇称（ungerade）模 IR 活性。因此，同一普通声子同时强 Raman 与 IR 活性，常被怀疑存在反演对称破缺或奇偶模混合。

    FePS₃ 的复杂性在于：122 cm⁻¹ 激发不是普通声子，而是磁性集体激发或与 Fe 3d⁶ 多重态相关的磁激发。磁激发的光学活性可通过自旋轨道耦合、交换 striction、磁偶极跃迁或自旋—声子耦合获得，因此不必严格遵循普通晶格声子的 Raman/IR 互斥图像。由于 FePS₃ AFM 态被认为保持反演对称性，同时出现 Raman 和 IR 信号仍是开放问题。

    为什么法拉第旋转能证明磁性激发？

    法拉第旋转来自左右圆偏振光在磁化或外磁场下传播相位/吸收不同。普通非磁声子在无自旋耦合情况下通常不会产生强磁场奇的旋光响应。122 cm⁻¹ 模在 ±7 T 下产生 0.1–0.15 rad 旋转，远高于 2 mrad 灵敏度，并随磁场劈裂，说明其与磁矩、Zeeman 能量或反铁磁共振密切相关。声子模也出现 Faraday rotation，则进一步说明这些声子通过自旋—声子耦合获得磁光活性。

    为什么光学谱能看到与中子散射不同动量位置的激发？

    理想光学实验中光子动量很小，只能激发 q ≈ 0 模；中子散射可测任意 q 的色散。文中 15 meV 和 40 meV 激发与中子散射能量相符，但中子报告的位置包含 commensurate 和 incommensurate q。可能机制包括：磁性单胞折叠使有限 q 模折叠到光学 Γ 点、磁有序降低平移对称性、缺陷/畴/有限尺寸放宽动量选择定则，或磁激发本身在相关 q 处具有可光学耦合的等效分量。该点仍需显微模型检验。

    ---

    第五部分：创新评估与关联（Synthesis & Novelty）

    1. 创新性判断

    从“看到磁激发”推进到“定量圆偏振光学响应”

    过去 2–5 年 FePS₃ 研究已通过 Raman、红外或中子散射识别 122 cm⁻¹ / 15 meV 磁激发及其磁场劈裂。但当前工作的新增价值在于结合绝对透射与Faraday rotation，重构圆偏振光学电导，直接观察场劈裂激发的二色性。这解决了前人较少触及的“磁激发对 σ⁺/σ⁻ 光的谱权重如何分配”的问题。

    首次系统给出 FePS₃ 偏振红外光学电导

    FePS₃ 的偏振透射和偏振光学电导被系统给出，尤其覆盖 40–4000 cm⁻¹、150 K 到 5 K 和两条主极化。该数据使声子各向异性、低温新增模式、900 cm⁻¹ 中红外特征和磁态光谱重构得以关联。相对非偏振谱，极化分辨数据能分辨 Aᵤ/Bᵤ 模式方向性和磁态下的各向异性响应。

    揭示 129 cm⁻¹ 附近磁振子—声子杂化的磁光证据

    上支磁激发在约 129 cm⁻¹ 处二色性减弱，与邻近红外声子杂化相一致。此前研究多关注 122 cm⁻¹ 模的 Zeeman 劈裂或 Raman 线形；这里通过圆偏振磁光响应显示混合后磁性权重改变，为磁振子—声子耦合提供了更直接的动力学证据。

    声子法拉第旋转提供自旋—声子耦合的新证据

    多个声子模出现显著 Faraday rotation，说明晶格振动在磁场和反铁磁序作用下获得光学活性。这超越了“声子频率在 Tₙ 附近异常”这类传统 spin–phonon coupling 证据，转向“声子携带磁光响应”的更强判据。

    发现磁态专属的宽中红外 900 cm⁻¹ 特征

    约 900 cm⁻¹ 宽吸收只在 Tₙ 以下出现且具有极化选择性，提示反铁磁态中晶格或电子—晶格响应重构。该特征为 FePS₃ 的磁相光谱指纹提供新增观测窗口，可能关联高阶声子、多声子过程、磁弹耦合或局域电子态变化。

    解决的前人缺口

    核心补足了三类缺口：

    • 磁激发与声子如何相互作用：通过 129 cm⁻¹ 杂化、声子 Faraday rotation 和极化依赖谱重构给出证据。
    • 磁激发圆偏振光学权重如何分布：通过绝对透射 + Faraday rotation 重构圆电导并显示二色性。
    • zigzag 反铁磁序如何影响晶格光学响应：通过 Pol. 1/Pol. 2 声子谱在 Tₙ 以下的强各向异性直接展示。
    阅读原文 ↗
    原文链接页内定位
  8. 08
    轻掺杂 LiₓCoO₂ 的反铁磁序与磁极化子#
    Antiferromagnetic order and magnetic polarons in lightly doped LiₓCoO₂ (x sim 0.9)#
    📊 含图深析
    🧭 物理 / 凝聚态📖 arXiv / cond-mat👤 Sudip Pal, Pampa Sadhukhan, Waqar Suleman, Andrej Pustogow, S. B. Roy🔥 AI 78

    💡 亮点：x≈0.9 的 LiₓCoO₂ 同时显现反铁磁序和磁极化子。

    📖 展开分析 + 配图
    研究问题轻微缺锂的层状 LiₓCoO₂（x≈0.9）中，Li 空位引入的少量空穴究竟形成普通顺磁自旋，还是会在三角 CoO₂ 层内局域成磁极化子，并进一步产生高温弱铁磁团簇与低温部分反铁磁有序；核心矛盾是室温以上仍有磁滞/热磁不可逆，而 10 K 附近又出现弱反铁磁异常。
    创新方法用多探针把分散现象拼成统一图像：SQUID 磁化、比热、⁷Li NMR 与 X-band EPR 同时追踪 Li 缺位—空穴局域化—CoO₆ 畸变—磁极化子扩散/冻结—团簇磁有序链条。Aha 点是：EPR 只看见约 1% 空穴的孤立小极化子，而绝大多数空穴可能合并成 EPR 静默的短程铁磁团簇；其中少量团簇在 T_N≈10 K 以下转入部分反铁磁有序。
    工作流程制备轻缺锂多晶 Li₀.₉₂CoO₂ → 用同步辐射 XRD/ICP-OES/热气萃取确认单相 Rbar3m 层状结构与 Li 缺位 → 低场/高场磁化测 ZFC-FC 分叉、M-H 磁滞与 10 K 驼峰 → 比热扣除晶格背景寻找 λ 型异常和磁熵 → ⁷Li NMR 记录 T₁⁻¹、线宽异常 → X-band EPR 解析 g≈2.14 窄线、200 K 线宽极小值和低温粉末谱 → 输出“高温磁极化子铁磁团簇 + 低温少量反铁磁团簇”的磁性相图。
    关键结果样品为单相菱方层状结构，成分约 Li₀.₉₂Co₁.₀O₂.₀₄。100 Oe 下 ZFC/FC 热磁不可逆持续到≈380 K，室温 M-H 有磁滞，指向高温短程铁磁相关。T_N≈10 K 附近，磁化出现弱宽驼峰，比热出现弱宽 λ 型峰且 9 T 下变宽下移，⁷Li NMR 的 T₁⁻¹ 与线宽同步异常。磁熵仅相当于总空穴约 7%，说明只有少量空穴团簇反铁磁有序。EPR 室温窄线 g≈2.12–2.14、线宽≈28 G，但只对应约 1% 总空穴，并在≈200 K 出现线宽极小值，对应极化子跳跃到冻结的交叉。
    应用价值揭示电池正极材料 LiCoO₂ 在轻微缺锂时并非磁性惰性，而会出现由 Li 空位控制的局域空穴、磁极化子、短程铁磁团簇和低温反铁磁团簇；为理解层状钴氧化物的绝缘输运、Li 扩散耦合磁性、EPR 异常信号和轻掺杂强关联行为提供实验框架，也提示可通过 Li 缺位浓度调控纳米尺度磁团簇。

    第一部分：核心概览（Overview）

    LiₓCoO₂（x≈0.9）中轻微锂缺位引发的磁性并非单一顺磁响应，而是由少量空穴形成的反铁磁有序团簇与磁极化子诱导的弱铁磁/短程铁磁团簇共同构成。体磁化、比热与⁷Li NMR 在 T_N≈10 K 附近一致显示宽而弱的反铁磁异常；低场磁化在最高 ≈380 K 仍存在热磁不可逆性，室温 M–H 曲线出现磁滞，指向高温短程铁磁相关。EPR 仅探测到约 1% 总空穴，其温度依赖可由磁极化子扩散/冻结解释。核心贡献在于把 Li 缺位、空穴局域化、Li 扩散、磁极化子与低温反铁磁序联系为统一图像，为理解层状钴氧化物中轻掺杂磁性提供了新证据。

    ---

    第二部分：结构化快速回顾

    《Antiferromagnetic order and magnetic polarons in lightly doped LiₓCoO₂ (x sim 0.9)》（None，）

    背景

    LiCoO₂ 是锂离子电池核心正极材料；x<1 时 Li 缺位引入空穴，可能使部分 Co³⁺ 转化为低自旋 Co⁴⁺（S=1/2）。轻掺杂区 0.9<x<1 的磁性、有无长程磁序、绝缘机制与极化子存在性长期未决。

    方法

    制备多晶 LiₓCoO₂，化学计量约 Li₀.₉₂(0.03)Co₁.₀O₂.₀₄(0.02)。采用同步辐射 XRD、ICP-OES、热气萃取、SQUID 磁化、PPMS 比热、⁷Li NMR（3–5.7 T，2–100 K）与 X-band EPR（ν=9.47 GHz，5–300 K）。

    结果

    XRD 显示单相菱方 Rbar3m 结构。低场 100 Oe 磁化显示 ZFC/FC 热磁不可逆性，可持续至 ≈380 K；ZFC 在 ≈200 K 有宽极小值，在 ≈10 K 有弱反铁磁样驼峰。比热在 ≈10 K 出现宽 λ 型异常，9 T 下变宽并向低温移动。⁷Li NMR 的 T₁⁻¹ 与线宽在 ≈10 K 附近出现异常。EPR 室温窄线 g≈2.12–2.14，linewidth≈28 G，但仅约 1% 空穴贡献信号。

    讨论

    低温反铁磁序只涉及少量掺杂空穴；高温弱铁磁与磁历史依赖来自磁极化子团簇。EPR 线宽在 ≈200 K 附近出现极小值，指向高温极化子热激活慢跳跃、低温跳跃冻结及局域各向异性 g 张量粉末谱。

    局限

    样品为多晶，难以解析方向依赖；EPR 只在 X-band 探测，绝大多数局域自旋“静默”；微观磁结构、极化子空间分布、团簇尺寸及 Li 扩散与磁性之间的因果链仍需中子、μSR、局域结构或更宽频谱实验确认。

    结论

    Li₀.₉CoO₂ 的磁响应由磁极化子主导：高温形成短程铁磁团簇并造成低场历史依赖，低温少量空穴团簇在 T_N≈10 K 以下进入部分反铁磁有序态。

    ---

    第三部分：逐章节冷凝解析（Section-by-Section Condensing）

    Abstract

    • Combined probes reveal partial antiferromagnetic ordering

    体磁化、比热与 NMR 共同探测到宏观磁响应中的低温反铁磁转变，转变温度约 T_N≈10 K。关键表述为 *"The dc magnetization, specific heat and NMR measurements, which probe the macroscopic response, indeed show that this compound partially undergoes an antiferromagnetic transition below T_N ∼ 10 K."* 这里的 partially 表明并非全体磁矩或全体掺杂空穴参与长程有序，而是部分体积分数或部分空穴团簇进入反铁磁态。

    • Weak ferromagnetic response persists above room temperature

    低场磁化存在明显历史依赖，且弱铁磁信号可延伸到室温以上。直接证据为 *"we observed a weak ferromagnetic response, which gives rise to the history dependence in magnetization measurements at low fields and is observed at temperatures above room temperature."* 这与简单 Curie 顺磁图像不相容，因为纯顺磁体系通常不会在室温 M–H 原点附近表现磁滞或 ZFC/FC 不可逆。

    • Magnetic polarons explain high-temperature ferromagnetic clusters

    高温弱铁磁被解释为掺杂空穴形成的磁极化子导致的铁磁团簇：*"We propose that there are ferromagnetic clusters at high temperatures due to the formation of magnetic polarons out of doped holes."* 该判断把 Li 缺位产生的空穴、局域晶格畸变和局域磁相关联系起来。

    • X-band EPR detects only a minority spin population

    X-band EPR 中只有总自旋的一小部分有响应，并呈现类 Curie 顺磁行为：*"In EPR measurements performed at the X-band frequency, only a fraction of the total spins contribute and show Curie-like paramagnetic behavior as reflected in the temperature dependence of the EPR intensity."* 这意味着大量磁性单元可能因交换展宽、慢弛豫、团簇化或频率窗口不匹配而 EPR silent。

    • EPR temperature evolution follows magnetic-polaron diffusion

    EPR 谱随温度变化可由极化子扩散理解：*"The temperature variation of the EPR spectra can be understood in the framework of the diffusion of magnetic polarons."* 这为后文 ≈200 K 线宽极小值与 ZFC 磁化极小值之间的对应关系提供解释框架。

    ---

    I Introduction

    • Technological and correlated-electron motivations converge in LiₓCoO₂

    LiₓCoO₂ 既是电池正极材料，又与金属-绝缘体转变、电荷/磁有序、热电异常及 NaₓCoO₂ 超导等强关联问题相关。核心背景表述为 *"LiₓCoO₂ is the primary cathode material in rechargeable Li-ion batteries"*，并且 *"other phenomena like the metal-insulator transition, magnetic and charge ordering, anomalous thermoelectric effects and the discovery of superconductivity in sister compound NaₓCoO₂ provided additional thrust to this field."*

    • Layered triangular CoO₂ planes create frustration-prone magnetic geometry

    晶体结构由 Li 层与边共享 CoO₆ 八面体层沿 c 轴交替堆叠，Co 在 CoO₂ 层中形成三角晶格。关键结构事实为 *"LiₓCoO₂ forms a layered structure with Li residing between layers of edge-sharing CoO₆ octahedra alternatively stacked along the c-axis"*，以及 *"Co atoms are arranged in triangular lattice and are therefore prone to geometrical frustration."* 三角晶格使反铁磁交换天然受几何阻挫影响，容易产生短程有序、团簇态或非均匀磁态。

    • Stoichiometric LiCoO₂ is a low-spin Co³⁺ band insulator

    x=1 时 Co 为形式 3+，晶场使 Co-3d 分裂为低能 t₂g 与高能 e_g，Co³⁺ 为低自旋 t₂g⁶e_g⁰，S=0，因而无局域自旋并呈带绝缘体。原文证据为 *"Co³⁺ exists in the low-spin t₂g⁶e_g⁰ configuration (S = 0), and the compound is a band insulator."*

    • Li deficiency introduces Co⁴⁺-like holes but ligand-hole character remains possible

    x<1 的 Li 缺位预期导致部分 Co³⁺ 转为 Co⁴⁺，低自旋 t₂g⁵e_g⁰，S=1/2，并在 t₂g 价带产生空穴：*"Li-ion deficiency is expected to result into partial transformation of Co³⁺ to Co⁴⁺ with t₂g⁵e_g⁰ electronic configuration (low spin state, S = 1/2) and also leads to creation of holes in the t₂g valence band."* 但 X 射线吸收和光电子谱暗示缺锂样品中可能存在氧空穴：*"X-ray absorption and photo-electron spectroscopy however gives indication towards oxygen-hole in Li-deficient samples."*

    • Magnetism and long-range order remain unresolved

    轻缺锂 LiₓCoO₂ 的核心未解问题是 Li 空位如何影响磁性以及是否存在长程磁序：*"Primarily, it is not understood how Li vacancies affect magnetism and whether there is a long-range magnetic order in this compound."* 既有 bulk magnetization、μSR、EPR、NMR、中子散射结果彼此复杂，产生多种解释，包括 *"temperature-dependent charge disproportionation (Co³⁺ → Co²⁺ + Co⁴⁺⁾, spin-state transition, spin fluctuations, or surface effects."*

    • Insulating behavior in lightly doped regime motivates polaron physics

    在 0.9<x<1 区间，轻掺杂绝缘行为也存在争议。由于单站点双空穴占据罕见，传统 Mott 机制未必主导：*"the onsite coulomb interaction of holes might not be a dominant factor, as the double occupancy of holes at a single site is rare."* 已提出两种可能：杂质态 Mott 绝缘与局域极化子形成，即 *"a Mott insulating state formed out of the impurity states has been suggested"*，同时 *"the possibility of localized polaron formation has also been proposed."*

    • Central objective links antiferromagnetism, weak ferromagnetism and magnetic polarons

    研究对象为轻微 Li 缺位多晶 LiₓCoO₂（x≈0.9），使用 bulk magnetization、heat capacity、NMR、EPR。关键结论预设为 *"a small fraction of the doped holes undergoes a magnetic transition to an antiferromagnetic state below T_N ∼ 10 K"*；高温低场历史依赖则被归因于弱铁磁，进一步解释为 *"weak ferromagnetism arises due to the formation of bound magnetic polarons, which can exist as nanoscale inhomogeneities formed out of doped holes."*

    ---

    II Experimental details

    • Polycrystalline synthesis used conventional solid-state reaction

    多晶 LiₓCoO₂ 通过固相法制备，原料为 99.99% 纯度 Li₂CO₃ 与 Co₃O₄，充分混合并多小时研磨，在 800 °C 加热 24 h，中间多次研磨。证据为 *"Stoichiometric amount of Li₂CO₃ and Co₃O₄ powders with a purity of 99.99% is thoroughly mixed"*，以及 *"the mixture was heated at 800 °C for 24 hours with intermediate grindings."*

    • Phase purity and structure were checked by laboratory and synchrotron XRD

    室温 XRD 使用 Rigaku Rotaflex RTC300 RC，18 kW rotating anode Cu-Kα 源；同步辐射 XRD 来自 INDUS-2, RRCAT Indore。结构精修使用 FullProf。关键方法表述为 *"The phase formation of the sample has been checked at room temperature in lab-based Rigaku Rotaflex RTC300 RC diffractometer with 18 kW rotating anode Cu-Kα x-ray source and analyzed by rietveld refinement using Fullprof software."*

    • Stoichiometry was independently determined for cations and oxygen

    Li 与 Co 含量用 ICP-OES，氧含量用热气萃取法，ICP-OES 仪器为 SPECTRO CIROS。证据为 *"we have used two different techniques, namely the ICP-OES ... to analyze Li and Co and the hot gas extraction method to determine oxygen content."*

    • Magnetization and heat capacity used commercial high-field platforms

    磁化在 7 Tesla SQUID-VSM MPMS3 上完成；比热在 9 Tesla PPMS 中用 relaxation method 测量，样品为单块 LiₓCoO₂ pellet，质量约 6 mg。证据为 *"Magnetization measurements have been carried out in 7 Tesla superconducting quantum interference device magnetometer"*，以及 *"Heat Capacity of a single piece of LiₓCoO₂ pallet weighing approximately 6 mg has been measured in the relaxation method using 9 Tesla Physical Property Measurement System."*

    • ⁷Li NMR covered low-temperature and multi-field regimes

    NMR 在 ⁷Li 核上进行，磁场范围 3–5.7 T，温区 2–100 K，位于 TU Wien 的 Quantum Design PPMS cryostat。弛豫率用 saturation recovery 方法确定：*"Nuclear magnetic resonance (NMR) measurements were carried out on ⁷Li nuclei at magnetic fields from 3 to 5.7 T ... covering a temperature range 2–100 K"*，以及 *"the relaxation rate was determined by the saturation recovery method."*

    • X-band EPR probed 5–300 K spin dynamics

    EPR 使用 Bruker EMX X-band 谱仪，频率 ν=9.47 GHz，温区 5–300 K，样品为单块多晶 pellet，连续流氦低温恒温器。记录吸收一阶导数 dP/dH：*"The EPR experiments in the temperature range between 5 and 300 K were performed using Bruker EMX X-band spectrometer at a frequency of ν = 9.47 GHz"*，以及 *"The first derivative of the EPR absorption spectra (dP/dH ... ) is recorded using a phase-sensitive lock-in amplifier detection technique."*

    ---

    III Experimental Results

    III.1 Sample details

    • Single-phase rhombohedral Rbar3m structure was obtained

    同步辐射 XRD 波长为 λ=0.7112 Å，所有衍射峰均可用菱方 Rbar3m 空间群索引，未见可探测二次相。证据为 *"All the observed reflections in the powder pattern can be nicely indexed by assuming a rhombohedral crystal structure with Rbar3m space group without any detectable secondary phase."*

    • Wyckoff positions match layered LiCoO₂ structure

    Li、Co、O 分别占据 3b、3a、3c 位点，氧 z 坐标可精修：*"The Li, Co, and O atoms occupy the Wyckoff positions 3b, 3a, and 3c, respectively, where the z coordinate of the position parameter of the oxygen atom is refinable."* 这支持标准 O3 型层状 LiCoO₂ 结构模型。

    • Refined lattice constants agree with literature

    精修得到 a=b=2.814 Å，c=14.051 Å，与既有报道一致。原文为 *"The lattice parameters obtained from the Rietveld refinements of the powder pattern are a=b= 2.814 Å and c= 14.051 Å, which are similar to the reported values in the literature."*

    • Chemical composition confirms slight Li deficiency

    化学计量为 Li₀.₉₂(0.03)Co₁.₀O₂.₀₄(0.02)，Li 含量低于 x=1，可能来自制备过程 Li 挥发。证据为 *"The composition of the LiCoO₂ with the general formula LiₓCo_yO_z is found to be x = 0.92(0.03), y = 1.0, and z = 2.04(0.02)."* 以及 *"The lower value of Li than expected (x = 1) is most likely due to evaporation of Li during sample preparation."*

    ---

    III.2 Magnetization and resistivity

    • Low-field M–T protocols reveal ZFC/FC history dependence

    在 μ₀H=100 Oe 下测量 ZFC、FCC、FCW。ZFC 为零场冷却至最低温后加场并升温记录；FCC/FCW 为同一磁场下随后的降温与升温。温度扫描速率分别为初始冷却 10 K/min、测量 1.5 K/min。证据为 *"M−T curve at μ₀H = 100 Oe measured in the zero field cooling (ZFC), field cooled cooling (FCC) and field cooled warming (FCW) protocols"*，以及 *"The temperature sweep rates during the initial cooling and the measurements are 10 K/min and 1.5 K/min, respectively."*

    • Magnetization is weakly temperature-dependent above 50 K but rises rapidly at lower temperatures

    M–T 曲线在 50 K 以上温度依赖较弱，低于 50 K 后迅速增大。直接表述为 *"All the curves are weakly dependent of temperature down to 50 K and rapidly increase at further lower temperatures."* 这表明低温出现额外磁响应，可能来自局域磁矩、团簇冻结或反铁磁相关增强。

    • Thermomagnetic irreversibility persists to about 380 K

    低场下 ZFC 与 FCW/FCC 之间存在有限不可逆性，并随温度升高逐渐减小，但一直延伸到测量最高温 T≈380 K。证据为 *"The most interesting observation is a finite thermomagnetic irreversibility between the ZFC and FCW/FCC curves"*，以及 *"The irreversibility gradually decreases with increasing temperature but persists till the maximum temperature of the measurements, which is T ∼ 380 K."*

    • FCC and FCW coincide, whereas ZFC differs

    FCC 与 FCW 无差异，说明场冷态在冷却/升温循环中较稳定；异常主要来自 ZFC 非平衡态。证据为 *"There is no difference between the FCC and FCW curves."*

    • Low-field irreversibility is suppressed by increasing magnetic field

    ZFC 与 FCW 分叉随场增强而被压制，在 μ₀H≈1 T 时两条曲线重合。证据为 *"The bifurcation between the ZFC and FCW curves gradually suppresses with an increase in the fields"*，以及 *"At μ₀H ∼ 1 Tesla ... two curves are identical as reported in the literature."*

    • ZFC curve has a broad minimum near 200 K

    ZFC 磁化随降温先缓慢下降，在 T≈200 K 附近达到宽极小值，然后在更低温迅速上升；FC 曲线则单调增加。关键证据为 *"the ZFC magnetization actually decreases slowly"*，*"It exhibits a broad minimum with the lowest magnetization around T ∼ 200 K"*，以及 *"the FCC/FCW curves monotonically increase down to the lowest temperature."*

    • A weak broad hump near 10 K resembles antiferromagnetic transition

    在 T_N≈10 K 附近，ZFC 曲线中可见弱而宽的驼峰，导数曲线中更明显。证据为 *"We see a weak and broad hump around T_N ∼ 10 K more clearly visible in the ZFC curve ... which resembles an antiferromagnetic transition."* 以及 *"This becomes more prominent in the derivative curve."*

    • Thermal cycling identifies ZFC as non-equilibrium

    通过 ZFC 与 FC 状态下逐步升高温度的热循环实验判断平衡性；只有 ZFC 状态在每次热循环后磁化单调增加，显示 ZFC 非平衡特征。证据为 *"We attempted to determine the equilibrium state of the system"*，以及 *"only in the ZFC state, the magnetization monotonically increases after each thermal cycle. This indicates the non-equilibrium character of the ZFC state."*

    • Room-temperature M–H hysteresis indicates non-paramagnetic magnetic state

    室温等温 M–μ₀H 曲线在原点附近显示磁滞，说明室温磁态不是纯顺磁，而存在短程铁磁相互作用。证据为 *"the isothermal magnetization measurements as a function of magnetic field ... at room temperature ... clearly show a hysteresis at the origin"*，以及 *"This also indicates that the magnetic state at room temperature is not purely paramagnetic and points towards the presence of short-range ferromagnetic interaction."*

    • Nearly linear high-field M–H suggests coexistence of isolated spins and weak ferromagnetism

    磁滞闭合后 M–H 近似线性增加，说明弱铁磁背景与孤立顺磁自旋并存。证据为 *"the M−μ₀H increases nearly linearly after the closure of the hysteresis loop"*，以及 *"indicates the co-existence of isolated spins showing paramagnetic response along with the weak ferromagnetism."*

    • At 2 K M–H remains similar but coercivity is reduced

    2 K 下 M–H 曲线也显示类似行为，但矫顽力减小：*"At 2 K, the M−μ₀H ... also shows similar behavior, however, with reduced coercivity."* 低温反铁磁相关可能改变铁磁团簇响应，使磁滞细节变化。

    • Li-ion diffusion freezing is relevant but insufficient alone

    先前研究观察到不同冷却速率下 ZFC-M(T) 曲线分叉，并与 ⁷Li NMR 中 Li 扩散减慢相关。关键背景为 *"the Li-NMR studies showed temperature dependence of the spin-lattice relaxation time, T₁, and the line width of the ⁷Li nucleus, which is due to the reduction of Li-ion diffusion with reducing temperatures."* 但单靠 Li 扩散冻结难以解释体磁化变化，因而提出磁极化子机制：*"we propose that the bifurcation between the ZFC and the FCW M(T) curves at low magnetic fields ... is related to the formation of magnetic polarons."*

    • Transport follows 3D Mott variable-range hopping

    电导率可用 Mott VRH 表达：σ=σ₀ exp[(T₀/T)^−p]，其中 p=1/(d+1)；样品数据符合三维 VRH，p=1/4。证据为 *"the conductivity using Mott’s VRH can be expressed as σ = σ₀ exp(T₀/T)⁻p, where p = 1/(d+1)"*，以及 *"the transport data ... can be fitted to Mott’s formula for 3-dimensions, with p = 1/4."* 半对数 σ vs T⁻⁰·²⁵ 为直线：*"A semi-log plot of σ vs T⁻⁰.25 gives a straight line."*

    ---

    III.3 Heat capacity

    • Zero-field heat capacity shows weak broad λ-like anomaly near 10 K

    无外场下测量至 T=30 K，比热在 T≈10 K 附近出现弱而宽的 λ-like anomaly，与磁化中反铁磁转变一致。证据为 *"Around T ∼ 10 K, a weak and broad λ-like anomaly is observed, which is likely associated with the antiferromagnetic transition, consistent with the magnetization measurements."*

    • Phonon background was modeled by βT³+γT⁵ between 20 and 50 K

    晶格比热通过 20–50 K 范围内拟合 Cₚₕ₌βT³+γT⁵ 估计，并外推到 2 K。证据为 *"we have fitted the total heat capacity in the temperature range between T ∼ 20-50 K by a polynomial equation ... Cₚₕ = βT³ + γT⁵ and then extended down to T = 2 K."*

    • Magnetic heat capacity was obtained by subtracting lattice contribution

    磁比热来自总比热减去 Cₚₕ：*"The magnetic contribution to heat capacity across the transition can be found by subtracting Cₚₕ from the total heat capacity."* 这一步用于量化参与磁有序的熵。

    • Magnetic entropy is extremely small: 0.035 K/mole K and 7% of hole doping

    转变释放的磁熵仅 0.035 K/mole K，约为估计 Li 缺位对应总空穴的 7%。证据为 *"The magnetic entropy released across the phase transition is only 0.035 K/mole K, which is only 7% of total hole-doping resulting from the estimated Li-deficiency."* 该数值强烈支持“部分有序”而非全体 Co⁴⁺/空穴有序。

    • Broad weak anomaly indicates antiferromagnetically ordered clusters rather than bulk full ordering

    无尖锐比热峰且熵很小，表明只有极少量掺杂空穴形成反铁磁有序团簇。证据为 *"The absence of a sharp specific heat anomaly and the small entropy indicates that only a very small fraction of the doped holes forms antiferromagnetically ordered clusters below T ∼ 10 K."*

    • 9 T magnetic field broadens and shifts the anomaly downward

    9 Tesla 下 λ 型异常进一步变宽，峰位略向低温移动。证据为 *"at 9 Tesla, the λ-like feature in the heat capacity further broadens, and the maxima of the peak position is slightly shifted towards lower temperatures."* 这符合常规反铁磁体在外场下转变被压低的行为：*"This is in line with the conventional antiferromagnetic state where the external magnetic field of a few Tesla suppresses the heat capacity anomaly by a few degrees."*

    ---

    III.4 Nuclear magnetic resonance

    • ⁷Li T₁⁻¹ follows approximately T² at lowest temperatures

    ⁷Li NMR 自旋-晶格弛豫率 T₁⁻¹ 在双对数图上低温近似 T²，高温斜率减小，40 K 以上变为亚线性。证据为 *"The log-log plot yields an exponent around T² at lowest temperatures, and its steepness reduces at higher temperatures, being sublinear above 40 K."*

    • Relaxation-rate bump slightly above 10 K supports antiferromagnetic order

    10 K 略高处出现 T₁⁻¹ bump，与磁化和比热推断的反铁磁序一致。证据为 *"there is a bump slightly above 10 K, which roughly coincides with the antiferromagnetic order deduced from magnetization and specific heat measurements."*

    • Single NMR resonance indicates small and relatively homogeneous spin density near Li

    所有磁场与温度下均为单一共振线，说明 ⁷Li 周围自旋密度较小且变化不大，因为未配对价电子主要位于 Co 离子上。证据为 *"The line shape is a single resonance at all fields and temperatures, reflecting that the spin density around ⁷Li nuclei is small and does not vary largely as the unpaired valence electrons reside primarily on the Co ions."*

    • No prominent line splitting across 10 K is expected from Li’s indirect coupling to Co spins

    通过 10 K 时没有显著谱线劈裂，虽然常规 AFM 转变可能导致内部场分裂。解释为 Li 位点附近自旋密度小。证据为 *"This is also the reason why no prominent line splitting is observed upon cooling through 10 K, as would be expected for an AFM transition."*

    • Linewidth increase confirms antiferromagnetic transition

    绝对线宽与相对线宽均显示明显增加，从而支持反铁磁转变。证据为 *"Still, a noticeable increase in line width confirms the antiferromagnetic transition, both on absolute ... and relative scales."*

    • Field dependence is weak from 3.0 to 5.7 T

    在 3.0、4.2、5.7 T 范围内，T₁⁻¹ 与 NMR 线宽没有显著场依赖。证据为 *"there is no significant field dependence in the inspected field range from 3.0 to 5.7 T, neither in relaxation rate nor in the NMR linewidth."*

    • Relative linewidth collapse indicates paramagnetic broadening

    线宽除以共振频率后不同场数据坍缩，说明展宽主要为顺磁性展宽。证据为 *"Normalizing the line width to the resonance frequency ... yields collapse of the data, indicating predominant paramagnetic line broadening."*

    ---

    III.5 Electron paramagnetic resonance spectroscopy

    • EPR is suited to local moments and spin dynamics without long-range order

    EPR 被用于研究缺乏长程磁序但具有局域磁矩和自旋动力学的体系。证据为 *"EPR ... is a useful tool for investigating magnetic systems lacking long-range magnetic order, especially those with local moments, spin dynamics."*

    • Room-temperature sharp EPR signal is anomalous for LiCoO₂ chemistry

    室温出现清晰窄 EPR 信号，其来源并不显然。原文强调 *"the origin of the well-defined and rather sharp EPR signal observed at room temperature is surprising and is not fully understood."* 化学原因是 Co³⁺ 低自旋无未配对电子，应 EPR 静默：*"Co³⁺ does not have any unpaired electron and therefore should be EPR silent."*

    • Observed room-temperature EPR parameters are g≈2.12–2.14 and linewidth≈28 G

    室温 EPR 窄线具有 g-factor≈2.12、线宽 28 G；后文又描述 Lorentzian 线在 g=2.14。证据为 *"we also have observed a sharp EPR signal at room temperature with a g-factor and linewidth of 2.12 and 28 G, respectively"*，以及 *"such a narrow EPR with a Lorentzian lineshape at g = 2.14 is surprising."*

    • g≈2.14 is compatible with Co⁴⁺ but most Co⁴⁺-like spins are not EPR visible

    g=2.14 与 Co⁴⁺ 期望 g 值吻合：*"the g = 2.14 matches well with the expected g value for Co⁴⁺ ion."* 但与 CuSO₄·5H₂O 标样比较显示只有约 1% 总空穴贡献 EPR 信号：*"only approximately 1% of the total holes is responsible for the observed EPR signal."* 因而 *"most of the localized spins in the system are EPR silent at the X-band frequency."*

    • High-temperature spectra above 100 K fit single Lorentzian line

    T≈100 K 以上 EPR 信号可用单一 Lorentzian 线型描述：*"The signal above T ∼ 100 K can be modeled assuming a single Lorentzian lineshape."* 这对应较快运动或较均匀局域环境导致的运动窄化。

    • Below 100 K spectra distort and below 40 K multiple lines emerge

    低于 100 K 后谱形逐渐畸变，单吸收线拟合不再充分；低于 40 K 出现额外谱线。证据为 *"at lower temperatures, the spectra undergoes a gradual distortion, which can not be satisfactorily modeled by a single absorption line"*，以及 *"below T ∼ 40 K, additional lines are clearly visible."*

    • Below 25 K EPR becomes complex due to additional lines

    T<25 K 时额外 ESR 线清楚可见，并在更低温增强，5 K 达到复杂吸收形态。证据为 *"At further lower temperatures, approximately T < 25 K, additional ESR lines are clearly visible and becomes prominent at further lower temperatures, resulting into a complex ESR absorption at the lowest measured temperature of T = 5 K."*

    • EPR intensity rises on cooling and has an anomaly near 200 K

    EPR 强度由双积分获得，正比于 EPR 中心静态磁化率。高温缓慢增加，低温迅速增加，并在 Tₘᵢₙ≈200 K 处有弱异常。证据为 *"To estimate the intensity, we have double integrated the spectra at individual temperatures"*，*"the intensity, which is proportional to the static susceptibility of EPR centers, slowly increases at higher temperatures and increases rapidly at lower temperatures"*，以及 *"we can identify a temperature scale Tₘᵢₙ ∼ 200 K, where the intensity shows a weak anomaly."*

    • EPR anomaly matches ZFC magnetization minimum

    Tₘᵢₙ≈200 K 与低场 ZFC 曲线宽极小值温度一致：*"This matches the temperature where a broad minima is observed in ZFC curve at low fields."* 这一温度对应极化子运动从热激活跳跃向冻结转变的交叉区域。

    • EPR linewidth has a minimum near 200 K and increases on both sides

    线宽随降温先减小，在 Tₘᵢₙ≈200 K 附近出现极小值，随后低温近似线性增大。证据为 *"The EPR linewidth gradually reduces, goes through a minima around Tₘᵢₙ ∼ 200 K and increases quite linearly at further lower temperatures."*

    • g-factor decreases and stabilizes near the same scale

    g 因子缓慢下降，并在类似温标附近趋于稳定：*"The g-factor slowly decreases and appears to achieve a stable value similar temperature scale."*

    • Isolated small polarons are proposed as EPR centers

    EPR 信号被归因于孤立小极化子：*"We propose that EPR signal appears from isolated small polarons."* 高于 Tₘᵢₙ≈200 K 时，极化子发生热激活慢跳跃，使线宽随温度升高而增大：*"Above Tₘᵢₙ ∼ 200 K, there is a thermally activated slow hopping of the polarons, which results into increasing EPR linewidth with increasing temperature."*

    • Low-temperature linewidth increase reflects hopping freeze-out and localized anisotropic g tensor

    低于 Tₘᵢₙ 后极化子跳跃逐渐冻结，线宽随降温再次增加；极低温出现局域极化子的各向异性 g 张量粉末谱。证据为 *"Below Tₘᵢₙ, the hopping gradually freezes and the linewdith increases again with decreasing temperature"*，以及 *"At very low temperature, we finally see the powder pattern arising from a localised polarons with anisotropic g-tensor."*

    ---

    IV Discussion

    • Li deficiency introduces localized holes bound to distorted Co⁴⁺O₆ octahedra

    Li 缺位引入空穴，已有软 X 射线谱显示局域空穴束缚在畸变 Co⁴⁺O₆ 八面体上，支持极化子形成。证据为 *"Li-ion deficiency introduces holes in the system"*，以及 *"Previous soft X-ray spectroscopy measurements revealed that the localized holes are bound to the Co⁴⁺O₆ distorted octahedra, and suggested formation of polarons."*

    • First-principles work allows ferro- or antiferromagnetically coupled polarons

    既有第一性原理计算提出极化子之间可铁磁或反铁磁耦合：*"First-principle calculation further proposed ferromagnetically or anti-ferromagnetically coupled polarons."* 这为实验中高温短程铁磁与低温部分反铁磁共存提供理论可能性。

    • Small polarons reside near Li vacancies and distort CoO₆ octahedra

    局域空穴通过畸变周围 CoO₆ 八面体形成小极化子，并靠近 Li 空位：*"The localized holes distort it’s surrounding CoO₆ octahedra to form small polarons and reside close to the Li vacancies."* 这解释了为何 Li 扩散与磁响应耦合。

    • Magnetization, heat capacity and EPR support short-range ferromagnetic polaron clusters

    体磁化、比热和 EPR 共同支持小极化子在掺杂空穴小团簇中产生短程铁磁相互作用，从而导致甚至室温下的历史依赖。证据为 *"small polarons give rise to short-range ferromagnetic interaction in small clusters of doped holes which in turn giving rise to history dependence in magnetization measurements even at room temperatures."*

    • Analogy with lightly hole-doped LaCoO₃ strengthens magnetic-polaron interpretation

    轻空穴掺杂 LaCoO₃ 中 Co³⁺ 低温保持低自旋非磁绝缘，但 La³⁺ 被 Sr²⁺/Ca²⁺ 替代后形成磁极化子与富空穴铁磁团簇。证据为 *"In lightly hole doped LaCoO₃, where Co³⁺ remains in low spin state at low temperatures and hence is non-magnetic and insulator"*，以及 *"replacing La³⁺ by Sr²⁺ or Ca²⁺ results into magnetic polaron formation and hole-rich ferromagnetic clusters."*

    • High-temperature state is mixed: ferromagnetic polaron clusters plus isolated holes

    Li₀.₉CoO₂ 的高温磁态包含两类成分：短程铁磁极化子团簇和 CoO₆ 八面体上的孤立空穴。证据为 *"the high-temperature magnetic state of Li₀.9CoO₂ comprises of a kind of mixed state containing both polaron clusters with short-range ferromagnetic interaction and isolated holes at CoO₆ octahedra."*

    • Low-temperature antiferromagnetism involves only part of hole clusters

    低温并非所有空穴团簇有序，只有部分空穴团簇在 T_N≈10 K 以下发生反铁磁转变。证据为 *"At low temperatures, some fraction of the hole clusters also undergo an antiferromagnetic transition below T_N ∼ 10 K."*

    • Microscopic details remain unresolved

    微观结构仍需进一步实验，尤其是极化子尺寸、空间分布、团簇磁结构与 Li 扩散耦合。限制性表述为 *"Nevertheless, further experiments are necessary to completely understand the microscopic details."*

    • Possible general trend in lightly hole-doped cobalt oxides

    与 LaCoO₃ 类比提示轻空穴掺杂钴氧化物中磁极化子可能具有普遍性：*"our study indicates towards a general trend in lightly hole-doped Co-based oxides."*

    • NaₓCoO₂ becomes relevant due to superconductivity and EPR resemblance to cuprates

    NaₓCoO₂ 因超导性值得比较，尤其 EPR 参数温度依赖与高 T_c 铜氧化物相似。证据为 *"it may be worthwhile to investigate NaₓCoO₂ which also shows superconductivity"*，以及 *"the uncanny resemblance of the temperature dependence of EPR parameters with high-T_c cuprates."*

    • EPR linewidth minimum resembles three-spin-polaron behavior in cuprates

    EPR 线宽中的明显极小值类似铜氧化物中三自旋极化子（TSP）的 EPR 线宽温度依赖。证据为 *"the distinct minima that is observed in the linewidth ... closely resembles the temperature dependence of the EPR linewidth in cuprates"*，以及 *"one hole at oxygen and two holes in adjacent Cu forms a quasi-particle, called as the three-spin-polarons (TSP)."*

    • Three-spin-polaron analogy links oxygen holes and neighboring transition-metal spins

    Emery 与 Reiter 的 TSP 模型中，氧空穴与两个邻近 Cu 空穴耦合形成准粒子，基态为自旋双重态。证据为 *"Emery and Reiter proposed a model for the superconductivity in terms of the so-called three-spin-polaron"*，*"This forms out of an oxygen hole coupled to two neighboring copper holes"*，以及 *"The ground state of such three-spin-polarons were found to be a spin doublet."*

    • Polaron mobility may be linked to Li-ion vacancy diffusion

    高温下，TSP 类极化子可随 Li 离子通过空位扩散而在 CoO₂ 层中经隧穿过程运动：*"At high temperatures, the TSP can move through the CoO₂ layer by tunneling processes as Li ions diffuse through the vacancies."* 极化子浓度应依赖 Li 空位浓度：*"The concentration of the polarons should depend on the concentration of the Li-ion vacancies."*

    • High local polaron concentration may form EPR-silent ferromagnetic clusters

    局部极化子浓度足够高时，可合并成具有局域铁磁相关的宏观团簇或液滴，且这些团簇可能 EPR 静默；这解释了 EPR 活性自旋比例极小。证据为 *"at high enough local concentration of the polarons, they may merge to give rise to macroscopic clusters or drops with local ferromagnetic correlation"*，以及 *"which will be EPR silent and hence consistent with the small amount of EPR active spins in the system."*

    ---

    V Summary

    • Li-deficient LiₓCoO₂ shows broad-temperature history-dependent magnetization

    样品为 Li 缺位 LiₓCoO₂（x≈0.9），低场磁化在宽温区存在历史依赖，并且室温仍有弱铁磁。证据为 *"Li deficient LiₓCoO₂ (x ∼ 0.9)"*，以及 *"this compound shows history-dependent magnetization at low fields in a wide temperature range and a weak ferromagnetism even at room temperature."*

    • Partial antiferromagnetic order appears below T_N≈10 K

    磁化与比热均显示宽而弱的驼峰，可能源于 T_N≈10 K 以下部分反铁磁有序。证据为 *"magnetization and heat capacity shows a broad and weak hump possibly due to partial antiferromagnetic order below T_N ∼ 10 K."*

    • Magnetic response is primarily driven by magnetic polarons linked to Li diffusion

    磁响应主因被归结为磁极化子形成，并与高温 Li 扩散密切相关。证据为 *"the magnetic response of this compound primarily driven by the formation of magnetic polarons which is intricately linked to Li diffusion at high temperatures."*

    • EPR suggests high-temperature three-spin-polaron-like entities

    历史依赖弱铁磁与温度依赖 EPR 共同指向类似高温超导体中的三自旋极化子。证据为 *"The history dependence of magnetization resembling weak ferromagnetism and temperature-dependent EPR spectroscopy suggest the three-spin-polarons at higher temperatures similar to high-temperature superconductors."*

    ---

    VI Acknowledgment

    • Experimental and technical support involved heat capacity, ESR, synchrotron XRD and stoichiometry measurements

    热容与 ESR 测量得到 Eva Brucher 帮助；同步辐射 XRD 得到 RRCAT 的 Archana Sagdeo 支持；Cu-Kα XRD 得到 N. P.     ---

    第四部分：深度理解与语言支持（Understanding & Nuance）

    1. 术语解析

    Magnetic polaron（磁极化子）

    指一个电荷载流子（这里主要是 Li 缺位引入的空穴）局域化后，通过与周围晶格和自旋背景耦合，形成携带局域磁畸变的复合准粒子。这里的磁极化子不是单纯“一个 Co⁴⁺ 自旋”，而是空穴、CoO₆ 八面体畸变、邻近磁相关和 Li 空位共同构成的局域对象。表达 *"localized holes distort it’s surrounding CoO₆ octahedra to form small polarons and reside close to the Li vacancies"* 强调了晶格畸变与 Li 空位邻近性。

    Thermomagnetic irreversibility（热磁不可逆性）

    指 ZFC 与 FC 磁化曲线在同一温度、同一磁场下不重合。它通常说明体系存在能垒、团簇冻结、玻璃态、磁畴效应或非平衡态。这里不可逆性延伸至 ≈380 K，并在 1 T 附近被抑制，说明低场弱铁磁/团簇态对磁历史敏感。

    EPR silent（EPR 静默）

    并不等于“没有自旋”，而是指这些自旋在给定 EPR 频率和实验窗口下无法产生可分辨共振信号。可能原因包括强交换耦合导致线宽过宽、团簇内弛豫过快、磁各向异性强、能级劈裂不匹配、或磁性团簇响应不符合 X-band EPR 条件。这里 约 99% 空穴不贡献 X-band EPR 信号，但仍可通过磁化和比热参与整体磁响应。

    λ-like anomaly（λ 型异常）

    比热在相变附近出现类似希腊字母 λ 的峰形。尖锐 λ 峰通常对应较清晰的二级相变；这里异常“weak and broad”，说明相变不是均匀全体相变，而更像分布式、团簇化、短程有序或体积分数较小的有序过程。

    Variable range hopping, VRH（变程跳跃）

    局域态中载流子通过不同距离、不同能量差的跳跃导电。Mott 三维 VRH 的特征是 lnσ 与 T⁻¹/⁴ 线性。这里 VRH 与极化子图像相容：空穴不是形成普通金属能带，而是在局域态之间跳跃。

    ---

    2. 疑难查证：几个复杂概念的高阶解释

    为什么只有 7% 空穴参与反铁磁熵释放，却仍能看到 T_N≈10 K？

    比热测到的是整个样品的热力学响应。若所有 Li 缺位产生的空穴都形成 S=1/2 磁矩并参与长程反铁磁有序，磁熵应接近按空穴浓度估算的较大比例。但实际磁熵只有估计空穴总量的 7%，说明反铁磁转变只发生在少数区域或少数团簇中。磁化和 NMR 仍能看到 T_N，是因为局部有序即使体积分数小，也会在低温产生可测的磁化斜率变化、比热宽峰和 NMR 线宽异常。

    为什么室温弱铁磁与低温反铁磁可以共存？

    体系不是均匀磁体，而是空间非均匀的轻掺杂体系。Li 空位分布、空穴局域化、极化子浓度波动会产生不同局域磁环境。空穴浓度较高的局部区域可形成短程铁磁极化子团簇；另一部分团簇或极化子在低温经不同交换路径形成反铁磁相关。因而“室温弱铁磁”与“10 K 部分反铁磁序”不是同一均匀自旋系统的矛盾行为，而是不同磁性组分在不同温区的响应。

    为什么 EPR 只看到约 1% 空穴？

    X-band EPR 的频率约 9.47 GHz，对应特定能量尺度和弛豫时间窗口。孤立、弱耦合、运动适中的小极化子容易给出窄 Lorentzian 信号；但如果极化子合并成铁磁团簇，内部交换强、线宽大、弛豫快，信号可能宽到不可见或偏离共振条件。因而 EPR 强度低不是否定磁性，而是说明可被 X-band 检出的只是少数孤立极化子。

    ≈200 K 极小值为什么重要？

    ZFC 磁化和 EPR 线宽/强度都在 Tₘᵢₙ≈200 K 附近出现异常。这个温标可能对应极化子运动状态的交叉：高于该温度，极化子随 Li 空位相关的动态环境发生热激活慢跳跃，运动导致 EPR 线宽随升温增大；低于该温度，跳跃逐渐冻结，局域环境不均匀和各向异性增强，线宽再次增大。ZFC 磁化极小值反映同一动态冻结过程对低场磁响应的影响。

    ---

    第五部分：创新评估与关联（Synthesis & Novelty）

    1. 创新性判断

    把轻缺锂 LiₓCoO₂ 的低温反铁磁异常与高温弱铁磁统一到磁极化子框架中

    近年相关工作已分别讨论 LiCoO₂ 中的 Li 扩散、空穴局域化、小极化子、磁异常或 EPR 信号，但低温 T_N≈10 K 反铁磁特征、高温至室温以上的低场磁历史依赖、室温 M–H 磁滞、EPR 中 ≈1% 空穴可见性 与 ≈200 K 动态异常，很少被放在同一物理图像中。这里的创新点是提出：

    Li 缺位 → 局域空穴/小极化子 → 短程铁磁团簇与孤立极化子共存 → 少量团簇低温反铁磁有序 → EPR 只探测孤立极化子。

    提供“部分反铁磁有序”的多探针证据链

    单一磁化驼峰容易被解释为杂质、顺磁尾或玻璃态；比热异常单独又可能因熵太小而显得可疑。多探针一致性增强了结论：

    • 磁化：T_N≈10 K 弱宽驼峰；
    • 比热：≈10 K 弱宽 λ 型异常，9 T 下变宽并下移；
    • NMR：T₁⁻¹ bump 与线宽 kink/增加；
    • 熵：仅 7% 空穴参与，解释异常弱而宽。

    这种证据链比单纯报告低温磁化异常更有说服力。

    将 EPR 可见自旋比例定量压低到约 1%，支持团簇/极化子非均匀性

    与 CuSO₄·5H₂O 标样比较得到 EPR 活性中心约占总空穴 1%，这是关键定量约束。它迫使解释不能把所有 Co⁴⁺ 当作等价孤立 S=1/2 中心，而必须引入 EPR 静默的团簇、强耦合区域或动力学窗口效应。

    把 Li 扩散与磁极化子动力学联系起来

    过去 Li 扩散冻结可解释 NMR 线宽或 T₁ 变化，但如何影响 bulk magnetization 不清晰。这里通过磁极化子给出桥梁：空穴极化子靠近 Li 空位，Li 空位扩散影响极化子运动；极化子运动/冻结改变短程铁磁团簇和低场历史依赖。这个联系尤其体现在 ≈200 K：ZFC 磁化极小值与 EPR 线宽极小值出现在相近温标。

    提出与三自旋极化子和高 T_c 铜氧化物的类比

    EPR 线宽温度依赖与铜氧化物三自旋极化子模型相似，提示层状钴氧化物中可能存在类似“氧空穴 + 邻近过渡金属自旋”的复合准粒子。这一类比并未被完全证明，但具有启发性，尤其考虑 NaₓCoO₂ 的超导背景。

    解决的前人问题

    至少推进了三个长期未解问题：

    • Li 缺位是否产生磁有序？

    结果支持少量空穴团簇在 T_N≈10 K 以下部分反铁磁有序。

    • 室温 EPR 窄线为何存在？

    结果倾向于孤立小极化子，而非简单杂质或全部 Co⁴⁺ 自旋。

    • 高温低场磁历史依赖从何而来？

    结果将其归因于磁极化子形成的短程铁磁团簇，并与 Li 扩散动力学耦合。

    仍需验证的新颖假说

    最具探索性的部分是“三自旋极化子”类比与极化子扩散图像。现有证据主要来自 EPR 线宽/强度温度依赖、VRH 输运、磁化历史效应与既有文献类比；还需要单晶 EPR、频率依赖 EPR、μSR、中子散射、局域结构谱学或实空间成像来确认极化子形态、尺寸、运动路径和磁耦合符号。
